### [89] [Evolutionary Discovery of Developmental Reward Schedules in Deep Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20858)
*Alan Nadelsticher Ruvalcaba*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种进化框架，用于发现强化学习中的发育型奖励调度，通过时间可变权重组合代理、新颖性和反应性三种生物启发的动机成分。在两个稀疏奖励的MiniGrid任务中，评估了四种进化算法（CMA-ES、xNES、DE、L-SHADE）与外部激励基线及三种手工设计方法的性能。结果表明，所有演化方法在DoorKey-6x6任务上均优于非演化基线，其中L-SHADE表现最佳，相对提升约11.4%；而在KeyCorridorS3R1任务上，仅CMA-ES表现良好，其余方法泛化能力较弱且不稳定。值得注意的是，发现的奖励调度与预设的发展顺序不同，新颖性在训练早期始终占主导地位。研究显示进化优化在深度强化学习中具有潜力，且计算环境下的最优解可能不同于生物学中的最优解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统强化学习中的奖励结构通常人为设计且固定不变，限制了动机优先级的动态演变。本文旨在探索通过进化方法自动发现随时间变化的奖励调度，以更自然地模拟生物发育过程中的动机演化。

Method: 提出一种基于进化算法的框架，利用CMA-ES、xNES、DE和L-SHADE等算法优化三个生物启发动机成分（代理、新颖性、反应性）的时间可变权重，实现动态奖励调度。在两个稀疏奖励的MiniGrid环境中进行实验验证。

Result: 在DoorKey-6x6任务中，所有演化方法均优于基线，L-SHADE表现最佳（相对提升约11.4%）；在KeyCorridorS3R1任务中，仅CMA-ES表现良好，其他方法泛化能力差。有趣的是，新颖性在训练初期始终占据主导地位，与预设发展顺序不符。

Conclusion: 进化优化是发现深度强化学习中发育型奖励调度的有前景方法，且计算环境下的最优奖励结构可能与生物演化所偏好者存在差异。

Abstract: The temporal structure of reward composition in reinforcement learning (RL) is typically hand-designed and held fixed throughout training, leaving the progression of motivational priorities largely unexplored. In this work, we propose an evolutionary framework for discovering developmental reward schedules, in which three distinct biologically inspired motivational components -- agency, novelty, and reactivity -- are combined through time-varying weights that dynamically shift over the course of training. Evaluated on two sparse-reward MiniGrid tasks: DoorKey-6x6 and KeyCorridorS3R1, our framework compares the generalizability of four evolutionary algorithms: CMA-ES, xNES, DE, and L-SHADE against an extrinsically motivated baseline (our main comparison point), and three additional hand-designed methods. On DoorKey-6x6, all evolved methods outperform the non-evolved baselines, with L-SHADE achieving the best performance -- an approximate relative mean improvement of 11.4% over the extrinsic only baseline. On KeyCorridorS3R1, CMA-ES achieves the best overall performance, with the remaining evolved methods showing weaker and less reliable generalization capability compared to the extrinsic only baseline. Interestingly, the discovered schedules diverge from our defined developmental ordering, with novelty consistently emerging as the dominant early signal during training, across both tasks. Collectively, our results position evolutionary optimization as a promising approach for developmental reward schedule discovery in deep reinforcement learning, and suggest that what evolution finds to be optimal in computational settings may differ from what it finds to be optimal in biology. The code for this project can be found at: https://github.com/alannadels/Evolutionary_RL.git.

Abstract: Cryopathy syndromes are difficult to classify because laboratory patterns often overlap across diagnostic categories, while some diagnoses are rare. This makes routine interpretation of cryoglobulin-related tests challenging and increases dependence on expert judgment. The aim of this study was to develop and compare machine learning approaches for automated classification of cryopathy syndromes from laboratory data and to identify a practical strategy for clinical decision support. Methods: We analysed laboratory records from 2,686 patients assigned to 14 diagnostic categories. The dataset included demographic variables, cryoglobulin measurements, precipitation tests, and hemagglutinin and hemolysin titers. Performance was assessed using stratified train-test evaluation and stratified 5-fold cross-validation. The main metrics were macro-averaged F1 score, accuracy, Top-3 accuracy, and expected calibration error. The overall task proved difficult because of marked class imbalance and clinical overlap between diagnoses. The best multiclass performance was achieved by a soft-voting ensemble of Random Forest and Gradient Boosted Trees. Cross-validation confirmed stable performance for the balanced Random Forest model. Feature engineering improved discrimination, and the most informative predictors were derived cryoglobulin-based interaction features.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 合成表格数据在受监管领域中促进微观数据共享，但连续时间生成模型需在分析效用、披露风险与计算成本之间取得平衡。现有潜空间流模型虽具灵活性，但其理论等价性在有限步积分与显式计算预算下可能转化为实际行为差异，亟需实证研究以指导实践。

Method: 在七个真实数据集上对潜空间流模型进行系统实验，比较不同学习目标（速度、分数、噪声、后验匹配）、概率路径（OT与VP）、采样方法（ODE与SDE）以及不同积分预算下的表现，通过定量评估分析效用与披露风险，并基于结果提炼配置建议。

Result: 1）学习目标显著影响效用-风险平衡：速度与后验匹配提高效用，分数与噪声匹配降低披露风险；2）配置与采样策略影响性能：中点采样提升分布保真度，OT路径允许更早停止，实现计算节省；3）提出可操作的默认配置与实践指南，适用于受限条件下的模型选型。

Conclusion: 本研究为合成表格数据生成提供了实证依据与实用指导，表明学习目标、路径选择与采样策略共同决定模型表现，合理配置可在保证安全性的前提下优化计算效率与数据效用。代码与补充材料已公开。

Abstract: Synthetic tabular data enables microdata sharing in regulated domains, yet deploying continuous-time generative models requires balancing analytical utility, disclosure risk, and computational cost. Latent-space flow models are flexible, but theoretical equivalences across learning targets, probability paths, and sampling dynamics can translate into different behaviour under finite-step integration and explicit compute budgets. We present an empirical study of tabular latent flow models across seven datasets, evaluating velocity, score, noise, and posterior matching objectives under optimal transport (OT) and variance-preserving (VP) paths, ODE and SDE sampling, and varying integration budgets. Our contributions are threefold: (1) we show that the learning target largely determines the utility-risk operating regime, with velocity and posterior matching tending to yield higher utility, while score and noise matching tend to achieve lower disclosure risk; (2) we demonstrate that configuration and sampling choices shift performance, with midpoint often improving distributional fidelity and OT paths often tolerating earlier stopping than VP, enabling compute savings under fixed budgets or risk thresholds; and (3) we distil these findings into actionable defaults and practical configuration guidance to support pre-release model selection under disclosure risk and resource constraints. The code implementation and supplementary materials can be accessed in https://github.com/rulnasution/tabular-latent-flow/.

### [92] [Temporal Causal Prior-Data Fitted Networks for Panel Data with Learned Reliability Signals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20889)
*Shravan Talupula,Saurabh Sharma*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: TCPFN 是一种用于零样本时间因果发现的奠基模型，能够处理工业级时间序列中的时序动态、时变处理和未观测混杂因素。其核心贡献包括：(1) 联合预测无效应概率、混杂强度、可识别性、中介比例和因果模式的因果判断头；(2) 覆盖六种因果模式的混合训练先验；(3) 采用跨注意力掩码的离散令牌面板数据架构以防止跨时域泄露；(4) 基于 FAISS 的上下文选择与一步后验修正实现单 GPU 上工业规模的零样本推理。在 19 个基准数据集上表现优异，如 Tennessee Eastman（AUROC 0.96）、Causal Rivers（AUROC 0.98），并在真实工业数据上实现 1,275 变量规模的快速推理（6 小时），远超传统方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出 TCPFN 模型，结合因果判断头、多模式因果先验、离散令牌面板架构与跨注意力掩码机制，利用 FAISS 实现高效上下文检索，并通过一步后验修正支持零样本推理，实现高精度与可扩展性。

Conclusion: TCPFN 成功构建了一个具备可靠性信号输出、可零样本部署且具备工业级可扩展性的时序因果发现基础模型，显著优于现有方法，为大规模工业系统因果分析提供了新范式。

Abstract: Estimating causal effects in industrial time series requires handling temporal dynamics, time-varying treatments, and unobserved confounders. Existing causal foundation models (CausalPFN, CausalFM) operate only on static cross-sectional data; neural temporal methods (CRN, G-Net) require per-dataset training; and concurrent temporal-PFN proposals have not been demonstrated at industrial scale. None output explicit per-pair reliability signals alongside their CATE estimates.
  We introduce Temporal Causal Prior-Data Fitted Networks (TCPFN), a foundation model for zero-shot temporal causal discovery with learned reliability signals. TCPFN makes four contributions: (1) a Causal Judgment Head that jointly predicts null-effect probability, confounding strength, identifiability, mediation fraction, and causal regime; (2) a mixed training prior covering six causal regimes (independent, direct, confounded, mediated, time-varying confounded, feedback) plus CausalFM-style front-door and instrumental-variable priors; (3) a discrete-token panel-data architecture with cross-attention masking that prevents inter-horizon leakage; (4) zero-shot inference at industrial scale via FAISS-based context selection and one-step posterior correction.
  On 19 benchmark datasets across five domains, TCPFN achieves competitive zero-shot causal discovery: AUROC 0.96 on Tennessee Eastman, 0.93 on SWaT, 0.98 on Causal Rivers, 0.97 on CAUSRCA. The null detector reaches NullF1 0.94, AUROC 0.99. TCPFN scales to V=1,275 on a proprietary Kraft pulp-and-paper dataset in 6 hours on a single GPU; PCMCI, a CPU-only library, on a V=666 sub-panel of the same data took 81.5 hours, extrapolating by O(V^2) to ~12.5 days at V=1,275. TCPFN's top edges identify cross-subsystem causal relationships while PCMCI's surface within-instrument controller-measurement coupling -- a scalability case study.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: MMGNN 将分子图分解为原子类型对特定的重叠子图：MMGNN-2D 基于共价连接构建化学着色子图；MMGNN-3D 基于空间邻近性构建几何着色子图，并引入距离、角度和扭转描述符增强边特征。两者共享消息传递主干，通过原子级聚合与分子读出整合表示。

Abstract: Molecular message-passing neural networks commonly propagate chemically diverse interactions through a single graph, which may mix interaction-specific signals and require deep propagation to capture long-range effects. MMGNN-2D constructs chemical-colored subgraphs from covalent connectivity, whereas MMGNN-3D constructs geometric-colored subgraphs from spatial proximity and augments their edges with distance, angular, and torsional descriptors. Both variants apply a shared communicative message-passing backbone to each subgraph and combine the resulting representations through atom-wise aggregation and molecular readout. We evaluated MMGNN on five classification and three regression benchmarks from MoleculeNet using common scaffold splits and five independent runs. MMGNN-2D achieved the highest macro-average AUC-ROC of 0.838 across the classification datasets and the lowest RMSE on ESOL (0.803). MMGNN-3D obtained the highest mean AUC-ROC on BBBP (0.956) and the lowest RMSE on FreeSolv (1.793), indicating complementary strengths of topological and geometric representations. Structural and leave-one-out analyses further illustrate how the subgraph decomposition affects learned representations and atom-type-pair sensitivities. These results support overlapping interaction-specific graph decomposition as a competitive strategy for molecular property prediction.

Abstract: Iterative design and optimization of large, complex structures require fast and accurate prediction of stress, displacement, and other fields. Finite element analysis (FEA) is computationally expensive for this task. Existing neural network surrogates often struggle with varying topologies and complex boundary conditions. This study proposes the novel Dual-Stream Heterogeneous Graph Neural Network (DS-HGNN) for full-field stress and displacement prediction in thin-walled structures, demonstrated on box beams made of stiffened panels. DS-HGNN achieves the lowest stress and displacement RMSE compared with six benchmark heterogeneous graph neural network models. It also reaches comparable accuracy to the strongest benchmark models using 19%-38% fewer training samples. A targeted evaluation further shows that DS-HGNN captures yield and post-yield stress features.

### [95] [Short-Term Electricity Demand Forecasting for New England Using a Hybrid Transformer-XGBoost Framework with Weather, Calendar, and COVID-19 Indicators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20918)
*Reza Ghanavati,Behrooz Mosallaei*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究提出一种混合框架，结合Transformer编码器提取时间特征与XGBoost模型进行新英格兰地区日度电力需求预测。该框架整合了六座城市的气象数据、日历与节假日效应、自回归需求滞后项以及新冠疫情流行病学变量。通过Optuna进行超参数优化，并采用70/15/15的时间序列划分策略。混合模型在测试集上表现优异，RMSE为8,876 MWh，MAPE为2.05%，R²为0.906；而仅使用表格数据的XGBoost基线模型则分别为9,304 MWh、2.21%和0.896。差异经Diebold-Mariano检验不显著（DM = -1.126，p = 0.262）。消融实验显示，疫情相关特征提升了训练精度，但在测试集上具有不对称影响：移除后使混合模型RMSE恶化3.2%，而仅XGBoost略有改善1.2%。SHAP时间分析表明，8个疫情特征中有5个在后急性期测试集中排名高于疫情活跃期训练阶段，说明模型过度依赖已过时的疫情模式。研究揭示了时间有效性衰减是核心机制：疫情导致的行为改变在2020–2021年形成强信号，但到2022年中已适应完成，此后这些变量成为噪声并加剧过拟合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准确的短期电力需求预测对电力系统运行、能源市场规划和基础设施优化至关重要。现有方法在处理复杂时间序列特征（如天气、节假日、疫情等）时存在建模能力不足或动态适应性差的问题，尤其在重大社会事件（如新冠疫情）后，模型容易因过时信息产生偏差。因此需要一种能有效融合深度学习与传统机器学习优势，并具备动态适应性的混合框架。

Method: 提出一种基于Transformer编码器与XGBoost的混合预测框架。利用Transformer捕捉长期依赖和多源时间特征（包括气象、日历、节假日、需求滞后及疫情变量），再由XGBoost进行最终预测。采用Optuna结合树状结构帕尔森估计器进行超参数优化，共500次试验。使用时间顺序的70/15/15划分方式确保无数据泄漏。通过SHAP值分析模型解释性，并进行消融实验评估各输入变量的影响。

Result: 混合模型在测试集上达到RMSE 8,876 MWh，MAPE 2.05%，R² 0.906；XGBoost基线为RMSE 9,304 MWh，MAPE 2.21%，R² 0.896。Diebold-Mariano检验显示两者差异不显著（p = 0.262）。疫情特征虽提升训练性能，但测试阶段存在非对称影响：移除后混合模型性能下降3.2%，而基线略升1.2%。SHAP分析显示疫情特征在疫情结束后仍被高估，表明模型存在对过时模式的过拟合。

Conclusion: 本研究验证了混合模型在电力需求预测中的有效性，但揭示了疫情等外部事件特征随时间演化后的“有效性衰减”问题。当社会行为模式稳定后，历史疫情变量反而成为噪声，引发模型过拟合。未来模型应引入动态特征筛选机制或定期重校准，以应对外部冲击带来的长期偏移，提升预测的鲁棒性与时效性。

Abstract: Accurate short-term electricity demand forecasting is critical for reliable power system operation, energy market planning, and infrastructure optimization. This paper presents a hybrid framework combining a Transformer encoder for temporal feature extraction with gradient-boosted decision trees (XGBoost) for daily electricity demand forecasting across New England. The framework integrates meteorological observations from six cities spanning all six New England states, calendar and holiday effects, autoregressive demand lags, and COVID-19 epidemiological variables. Hyperparameter optimization uses Optuna with a multivariate Tree-structured Parzen Estimator over 500 trials, with a leakage-free 70/15/15 chronological train-validation-test split. The hybrid model achieves a test RMSE of 8,876 MWh, MAPE of 2.05%, and R-squared of 0.906. A tabular-only XGBoost baseline achieves RMSE of 9,304 MWh, MAPE of 2.21%, and R-squared of 0.896. A Diebold-Mariano test (Harvey-Leybourne-Newbold correction) confirms the 427.7 MWh difference is statistically indistinguishable from noise (DM = -1.126, p = 0.262). An ablation study reveals COVID-19 features improved training accuracy but had asymmetric test effects: removal degraded hybrid RMSE by 3.2% while marginally improving XGBoost-only by 1.2%. A SHAP temporal analysis shows 5 of 8 COVID features rank higher on the post-acute test set than during pandemic-active training, indicating the model over-applies learned pandemic patterns. These findings establish temporal validity decay as a central mechanism: behavioral disruptions drove a strong COVID-demand signal during 2020-2021, but adaptation was complete by mid-2022, leaving epidemiological features as noise amplifying overfitting to stale pandemic patterns.

### [96] [$Ω$: Operator-based Mixture Ensemble for Generative Assimilation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20920)
*Pouria Behnoudfar,Nan Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为$Ω$的可扩展框架，用于在部分观测的高维非线性系统中表征非高斯后验分布。该方法结合条件高斯代理建模、无监督得分学习和生成采样，通过解析方式恢复高维未观测分量，降低计算成本，并利用集合轨迹进行去噪得分匹配，无需真实后验样本，显著减轻学习负担。最终通过高斯混合表示重构完整后验分布，并使用退火Langevin采样迭代优化集合成员，验证表明其在具有间歇性和极端事件的湍流模型中持续提升后验精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法如集合卡尔曼滤波依赖高斯近似，在强非高斯后验下不准确；粒子滤波则存在严重可扩展性问题；基于得分的生成方法通常需要真实后验样本进行监督训练，但在实际应用中难以获得。因此亟需一种无需真实后验样本、可扩展且能准确刻画非高斯后验的方法。

Method: $Ω$框架包含四个核心步骤：1）使用条件高斯代理模型提供非线性非高斯基线近似并获得闭式条件后验；2）基于集合轨迹通过去噪得分匹配学习基线之外的残差偏差，实现无监督训练；3）采用高斯混合表示重构完整后验分布，捕捉多峰、偏斜和重尾特性；4）使用退火Langevin采样迭代优化集合成员，逼近目标后验。

Result: $Ω$在多个具有间歇性和极端事件的湍流模型上进行了验证，结果表明其能够有效提升后验估计的准确性，尤其在非高斯特征显著的场景下表现优越，同时保持良好的可扩展性。

Conclusion: $Ω$是一种高效、可扩展且无需真实后验样本的生成式数据同化框架，能够准确刻画复杂系统的非高斯后验分布，在高维非线性系统中具有广泛的应用潜力。

Abstract: Characterizing non-Gaussian posterior distributions in partially observed high-dimensional nonlinear systems remains a fundamental challenge in data assimilation. Ensemble Kalman filters rely on Gaussian approximations that can be inaccurate for strongly non-Gaussian posteriors, whereas particle filters suffer from severe scalability limitations. Recent score-based generative approaches improve posterior characterization but typically require supervised training with ground-truth posterior samples, which are unavailable in most practical applications. We introduce $Ω$ (Operator-based Mixture Ensemble for Generative Assimilation), a scalable framework that integrates conditional Gaussian surrogate modeling, unsupervised score learning, and generative sampling. The conditional Gaussian surrogate provides a nonlinear non-Gaussian baseline approximation while admitting closed-form conditional posterior distributions for the unresolved variables. First, $Ω$ exploits these closed-form conditional distributions to analytically recover the high-dimensional unobserved component, reducing computational cost and mitigating the curse of dimensionality. Second, $Ω$ learns only the residual discrepancy beyond an analytical baseline through denoising score matching using ensemble trajectories alone, eliminating the need for ground-truth posterior samples and substantially reducing the learning burden. Third, $Ω$ reconstructs the full non-Gaussian posterior distribution of both observed and unobserved variables via a Gaussian mixture representation, capturing multimodal, skewed, and heavy-tailed statistics. Finally, $Ω$ employs annealed Langevin sampling to iteratively refine ensemble members from the baseline toward the target posterior. $Ω$ is validated on several turbulent models with intermittency and extreme events, consistently improving posterior accuracy.

</details>


### [97] [Hierarchical Pooling for Sheaf Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20932)
*Dionisia Naddeo,Carlo Abate,Pietro Liò,Nicola Toschi,Filippo Maria Bianchi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为HiSP的层次化剪枝框架，用于在Sheaf神经网络（SNNs）中构建层次化表示。该方法基于局部谱粗化，通过将细粒度的茎值特征投影到簇内剪枝拉普拉斯矩阵的低频本征模式上，构建粗粒度的茎。该过程利用伽辽金算子在粗空间中表示细粒度剪枝能量，并分析了粗化带来的近似误差，包括截断损失和实现损失。此外，作者实现了兼容SNN的PyG版本，支持批处理、提升的剪枝拉普拉斯矩阵及层次化架构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有剪枝神经网络架构主要在固定图分辨率下运行，缺乏一种原则性的池化机制来构建层次化表示，限制了其对复杂结构关系的建模能力。因此需要一种能保持剪枝结构信息的层次化池化方法。

Method: HiSP采用局部谱粗化，通过将细粒度特征投影至簇内剪枝拉普拉斯矩阵的低频本征模式，构造粗粒度茎；利用共链级延拓映射，结合伽辽金算子将细粒度剪枝能量映射到粗空间；同时分离并分析由舍弃局部模式引起的截断损失与由投影算子近似导致的实现损失。

Result: 实验表明，该方法能够有效构建具有物理意义的层次化剪枝表示，在保留关键结构信息的同时减少计算开销；所提出的实现支持批处理、提升剪枝拉普拉斯矩阵及多层堆叠，适用于复杂图结构的层级建模。

Conclusion: HiSP为剪枝神经网络提供了一种可解释、可扩展的层次化池化机制，使模型能够在保持剪枝结构语义的同时进行高效表征学习，是当前剪枝神经网络向更复杂图结构建模迈出的重要一步。

Abstract: Sheaf Neural Networks (SNNs) generalize Graph Neural Networks (GNNs) by replacing scalar node signals with stalk-valued signals and by using restriction maps to measure compatibility across edges. Unlike standard graph diffusion, which encourages neighboring node features to become similar, sheaf diffusion promotes consistency through the restriction maps and can therefore model more general relationships between neighboring nodes. However, existing sheaf neural architectures mainly operate at a fixed graph resolution and do not provide a principled pooling mechanism for building hierarchical representations. In this paper, we introduce Hierarchical Sheaf Pool (HiSP), a sheaf-aware pooling framework based on local spectral coarsening. Given a partition of the graph, HiSP constructs each coarse stalk by projecting fine stalk-valued features onto the low-frequency eigenmodes of the cluster-internal sheaf Laplacian. These local modes define a cochain-level prolongation map, which allows the fine sheaf energy to be represented on the coarse space through a Galerkin operator. We further analyze the approximation induced by coarsening by separating truncation loss, due to discarded local modes, from realization loss, due to representing the projected operator as a coarse sheaf. Finally, we implement HiSP as a GNN pooling layer compatible with SNNs and provide a PyG implementation supporting batching, lifted sheaf Laplacians, and hierarchical architectures.

</details>


### [98] [Towards Robust Training in NNGPT AutoML Pipeline: A Loss-Optimizer Pairing Selection Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20933)
*Anton Abramochkin,Radu Timofte,Dmitry Ignatov*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究系统评估了18种损失函数与优化器组合（6种优化器×3种损失函数）在33个异构模型上的表现，覆盖6个图像分类数据集。结果表明，不存在通用最优的损失-优化器配对；Cross-Entropy配合Adam或AdamW表现最稳健；NGL仅在自适应优化器下有效，且对SGD不适用；Adagrad和Adadelta在固定超参下始终表现较差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AutoML中的损失函数与优化器选择对训练效果有显著影响，但现有方法缺乏针对异构架构池的系统性配对指导，亟需实证研究以确定最优组合策略。

Method: 采用源码级注入管道自动构建594个模型变体，固定超参数条件下对所有18种损失-优化器组合进行系统性实验，覆盖LEMUR异构架构池中的33个基线模型及6个数据集。

Result: 无单一配对在所有架构和数据集上最优；CE+Adam/AdamW最为稳健；NGL仅在自适应优化器下表现良好，与SGD搭配时性能下降明显；Adagrad和Adadelta在固定学习率下持续表现不佳。

Conclusion: 损失-优化器配对应根据模型结构与任务特性动态选择，建议在实际应用中优先考虑交叉熵与Adam/W的组合，并避免使用Adagrad和Adadelta于固定超参设置。

Abstract: The choice of loss function and optimizer is an important decision, that shapes further model training. Yet automated architecture search pipelines (AutoML) benefits significantly more from the optimal pairing selection and vice versa. This paper investigates whether a single recipe is sufficient for heterogeneous architecture pools, or whether the optimal pairing varies across structurally diverse models. We conduct a systematic empirical study of all $3 \times 6 = 18$ combinations of six optimizers (SGD+Momentum, Adam, AdamW, RMSprop, Adagrad, Adadelta), paired with three loss functions: Cross-Entropy (CEL), Negative Log-Likelihood (NLL), and the recently introduced genetically evolved NGL loss across the base models presented in LEMUR heterogeneous architecture pool on six image classification datasets (CelebA-Gender, CIFAR-10, CIFAR-100, ImageNette, MNIST, SVHN). The 18 loss-optimizer configurations are applied to each of the 33 compatible base architectures taken from the LEMUR pool, resulting in 594 variants that were generated fully automatically by a source-level injection pipeline and evaluated under fixed hyperparameters, ensuring that observed accuracy differences are attributable solely to the loss-optimizer pairing. Our results confirm that no single pairing is universally optimal. Cross-Entropy with Adam or AdamW is the most robust choice across architecture families and datasets. NGL is a competitive alternative to CEL on standard convolutional classifiers, but only when paired with adaptive optimizers; it degrades substantially with SGD or accumulation-based methods. Adagrad and Adadelta consistently underperform under fixed hyperparameters regardless of loss function, highlighting their sensitivity to learning rate tuning. These findings provide actionable guidance for loss-optimizer selection within NNGPT Framework.

### [99] [Learning through Internalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20937)
*Nikolaos Tsilivis,Nirmit Joshi,Marko Medvedev,Julia Kempe,Nati Srebro*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究神经网络系统如何通过权重吸收显式计算过程（即内化），并探讨其对学习的促进作用。重点分析Transformer模型如何内化思维链（CoT）标记来模拟半自动机，揭示哪些类别的半自动机更难内化，并指出内化的副作用——分布外性能逐渐退化。研究首次提供了成功的内化过程的可证明分析：针对奇偶性学习任务，简化的一层Transformer在显式CoT监督下先学习目标，随后在逐步移除CoT标记时内化自回归生成，直接计算奇偶性。该任务在无CoT监督下从数据中学习极为困难。最后讨论了内化学习与最近提出的正分布偏移现象的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索神经网络如何通过吸收显式计算过程（如思维链）实现内部知识编码，以提升学习效率；同时揭示该过程可能带来的泛化性能下降问题。

Method: 通过实验和理论分析结合的方式，研究Transformer模型在不同条件下对半自动机的内化能力，特别是基于思维链（CoT）标记的模拟行为；采用简化的一层Transformer模型进行奇偶性学习任务的可证明分析，验证内化过程的有效性。

Result: 发现某些半自动机类别更难被内化；内化过程伴随分布外性能的持续退化；成功证明了一层Transformer在奇偶性任务中可通过逐步去除CoT标记实现内化，从而直接计算结果；且该任务在缺乏CoT监督时难以学习。

Conclusion: 内化机制能有效提升模型在特定任务上的学习能力，但可能导致泛化性能下降；内化过程与正分布偏移现象存在关联，提示需权衡模型的内在表示与外部泛化能力。

Abstract: We study internalization processes, by which neural-network-based systems absorb an explicit computational procedure into their own weights, and how they facilitate learning. We investigate how transformers internalize the simulation of semiautomata by internalizing chain-of-thought (CoT) tokens, which classes of semiautomata are harder to internalize, and expose the flip side of internalization, that is, a progressive degradation of out-of-distribution performance. We then provide the first provable analysis of successful internalization: for the task of learning parities, we show that a simplified one-layer transformer provably first learns the target with explicit CoT supervision and then internalizes the autoregressive generation as CoT tokens are progressively removed, learning to directly compute the parity. This task is computationally hard to learn from data without CoT supervision. Finally, we discuss how learning through internalization relates to the \textit{Positive Distribution Shift} phenomenon recently introduced by~\citet{Med+26}.

### [100] [Grouped Query Experts: Mixture-of-Experts on GQA Self-Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20945)
*Vishesh Tripathi,Abhay Kumar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出GQE（分组查询专家）机制，在保持GQA的KV缓存优势的同时，通过路由器为每个令牌选择k个查询头专家，仅激活部分查询头，显著降低计算开销。在30B令牌预算下，参数量为250M时，GQE在下游任务中达到与全激活GQA相当的准确率，但查询头激活数量减半。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准密集注意力在长序列下计算成本高，且对所有令牌统一使用相同注意力头，忽略令牌难易度和信息量，造成计算浪费。因此需要一种更高效的注意力机制以减少冗余计算。

Method: 在分组查询注意力（GQA）基础上引入混合专家（MoE）结构，每个GQA组内通过路由器为每个令牌选择k个查询头专家，而键值头保持密集不变，从而仅减少活跃查询头的计算量。

Result: 在固定30B令牌预算下，250M参数规模模型中，GQE在下游任务中的准确率与全激活GQA基线相当，但查询头激活数量减少一半，显著降低计算开销。

Conclusion: GQE有效结合了GQA的缓存优势与混合专家的稀疏计算能力，实现了在保持性能的同时大幅降低查询头计算成本，适用于长序列场景。

Abstract: Self-attention is central to Transformer performance and is often the most expensive part of the Transformer at long context lengths because its pairwise token interactions scale quadratically with sequence length. Standard dense attention also applies the same set of attention heads to every token regardless of token difficulty or information content. This uniform activation can waste compute, especially as sequences grow longer and attention cost increases rapidly. We propose Grouped Query Experts (GQE), a mixture-of-experts layer on top of grouped-query attention (GQA). Within each GQA group, a router selects k query-head experts per token while all key-value (KV) heads remain dense and unchanged. Thus, GQE keeps the KV cache benefits of GQA and reduces only the active query-head computation. On a fixed 30B token budget at the 250M parameter scale, GQE matches the all-active GQA baseline in downstream accuracy while activating half the query heads per token.

Abstract: Dynamic average estimation is a critical problem in multi-agent systems, enabling agents to collaboratively estimate time-varying signals using only local information exchange. Traditional model-based approaches often face challenges related to convergence speed and sensitivity to network topology changes. This paper introduces a novel learning-based solution leveraging Gated Graph Neural Networks (GGNNs) for fast-convergent dynamic average estimation in a fully distributed manner. Taking advantage of the inherent structure of GGNNs, the proposed method models the estimation process as a distributed autoregressor, ensuring rapid convergence while maintaining stability. We incorporate a regularization term during training to enforce convergence guarantees and introduce an encoding-decoding mechanism to reduce communication overhead without sacrificing accuracy compared to standard GGNNs. Extensive numerical experiments demonstrate that our approach significantly outperforms conventional model-based estimators in terms of both convergence speed and precision, making it a promising alternative for multi-agent applications that require dynamic average estimation.

### [102] [Right Knowledge, Wrong Answer: Test-Time Steering for Temporal Fact Conflicts in Open-Weight Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20959)
*Elias Hossain,Sourav Saha,Umesh Chandra Biswas,Sanjeda Sara Jennifer*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究提出参数时间冲突（PTC）问题，即大语言模型在参数中同时存储过时和新事实，标准提示可能引发过时回答。为此，作者提出时间吸引子引导（TAS）方法，通过三个阶段的测试时干预，在不重新训练或外部检索的情况下，检测冲突、识别关键层并引导隐藏状态向新事实表示。在包含8,746条记录的跨五个维基数据关系的验证基准上评估了四种开放权重模型，单层激活修补实现了0.72-0.85的答案翻转率；端到端TAS解决了29-57%的PTC案例，同时保持非冲突查询85-99%的准确率，优于匹配的ITI基线，在四个模型中的三个表现更优。结果表明，推理时可选择性覆盖过时的参数知识。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在训练过程中可能同时学习到过时和新事实，但标准提示方式常导致模型输出过时信息，影响其准确性与可靠性。因此需要一种无需重新训练或外部检索的方法，在推理阶段有效解决此类时间性知识冲突。

Method: 提出时间吸引子引导（TAS）方法，包括三个阶段：1）检测潜在的时间冲突；2）识别对冲突有关键影响的网络层；3）通过激活修补技术引导隐藏状态朝向新事实表示，实现对过时知识的选择性覆盖。

Result: 单层激活修补在所有模型中实现0.72-0.85的答案翻转率；端到端TAS成功解决29-57%的参数时间冲突案例，同时在非冲突任务上保持85-99%的高准确率，显著优于匹配的ITI基线，尤其在三款模型中表现更优。

Conclusion: 该研究证明，大语言模型中的过时参数化知识可以在推理阶段被有效且选择性地覆盖，而无需重训练或依赖外部知识源，为提升模型时效性与准确性提供了新的可行路径。

Abstract: Large language models can store both outdated facts and newer superseding facts in their parameters, but standard prompting may still elicit the outdated answer. We formalize this problem as Parametric Temporal Conflict (PTC) and introduce Temporal Attractor Steering (TAS), a three-stage test-time intervention that detects likely conflicts, identifies a conflict-critical layer, and steers hidden states toward newer-fact representations without retraining or external retrieval. We construct an 8,746-record verified benchmark across five Wikidata relations and evaluate four open-weight language models from three families: Qwen-2.5-1.5B/7B, Mistral-7B-v0.3, and Llama-3.1-8B. Single-layer activation patching achieves answer-flip rates of 0.72-0.85 across all models. End-to-end TAS resolves 29-57% of PTC cases while preserving 85-99% accuracy on non-conflict queries, outperforming a matched ITI baseline on three of four models. These results show that outdated parametric knowledge can be selectively overridden at inference time.

### [103] [Is Our Benchmark Enough? An Analysis of Continual Learning for MLLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20961)
*Van-Tuan Tran,Shruthi Gowda,Merim Dzaferagic,Marco Ruffini*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文挑战了当前多模态大模型持续学习中依赖MLLM路由的假设，提出一种无需训练、无需重放的原型路由方法RePRo，可实现与MR-LoRA相当性能但计算成本更低。同时发现共享专家对持续学习无实质帮助。研究指出现有基准MLLM-CL存在任务高度可分、任务顺序固定等结构性缺陷，导致其更侧重孤立学习而非真正的持续迁移。因此提出未来基准应包含重叠任务流形、多任务顺序、细粒度领域漂移及兼顾前向迁移与保留能力的评估机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多模态大模型持续学习依赖复杂且昂贵的MLLM路由机制，而现有基准（如MLLM-CL）的设计缺陷使得评估结果可能误导对真实持续学习能力的判断，亟需重新审视评估范式并设计更合理的基准。

Method: 通过在MLLM-CL基准上对比分析，提出训练-free、replay-free的原型路由方法RePRo，利用冻结预训练特征与任务原型进行匹配；同时系统评估共享专家的有效性，并分析基准本身的任务可分性与任务顺序敏感性问题。

Result: RePRo在性能上媲美基于MLLM的路由方法，但计算开销显著降低；共享专家未能提升持续学习表现；现有基准因任务高度可分且任务顺序固定，导致评估结果易受单一课程影响，无法反映真实持续迁移能力。

Conclusion: 多模态大模型持续学习的评估不应依赖复杂的路由机制或共享专家；现有基准存在结构性偏差，未来应设计更具挑战性的基准，涵盖重叠任务、多样化任务顺序和细粒度领域变化，以真正衡量模型的持续迁移能力。

Abstract: Continual adaptation is essential for multimodal large language models (MLLMs) deployed across evolving domains, but the state-of-the-art MR-LoRA method highly relies on the assumption that a MLLM-based router is necessary to process complex multimodal inputs. This paper revisits this claim on the MLLM-CL benchmark and argues for two claims. \textbf{First}, routing does not require an MLLM: a simple training-free, replay-free ptotypical routing method (\textsc{RePRo}), uses frozen pretrained features and task prototypes to match the MLLM-based router of MR-LoRA at far lower computational cost. \textbf{Second}, shared experts do not improve continual learning for MLLMs, despite their theoretical appeal. We show that these findings arise from two structural limitations of MLLM-CL: (1) its tasks are \textbf{highly separable} in representation space, and (2) its fixed task order makes conclusions \textbf{sensitive to a single curriculum} rather than robust across diverse continual-learning trajectories. As a result, the benchmark primarily rewards learning in isolation rather than genuine continual transfer. This motivates a new design for future benchmarks of continual MLLM learning, with overlapping task manifolds, multiple task orders, fine-grained domain shifts, and evaluation protocols that reward forward transfer as well as retention.

### [104] [Formalizing Task-Space Complexity for Zero-Shot Generalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20967)
*Jung-Hoon Cho,Heling Zhang,Siqi Du,Roy Dong,Cathy Wu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究上下文动态系统中的零样本泛化，提出一种以性能为中心的定向任务差异度量——符号发散（signed divergence），该度量可上界源上下文到目标上下文的泛化差距。符号发散定义了ε-容差集，用于认证源策略类是否能泛化，并引出了任务空间复杂性的具体概念：使每个目标上下文的泛化差距不超过ε所需的最少源上下文数量。在性能局部平滑的假设下，容差集具有可认证的内/外球体及实例相关的体积界。在有限查询设置中，源选择问题转化为集合覆盖，贪心策略继承标准的H(n)近似保证。通过质量-弹簧-阻尼系统和非线性CartPole系统的实验验证，贪心选择在达到相同ε覆盖时所需策略数少于均匀或随机基线。本方法提供基于性能的任务相似性度量与构建可泛化控制策略的实际证书。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有策略在不同条件下往往过于保守或过于复杂，难以实现高效零样本泛化；亟需一种既能保证性能又具备理论保障的通用策略设计框架。

Method: 引入符号发散作为任务间差异的度量，基于其构建ε-容差集以评估泛化能力；在局部平滑假设下推导出可认证的几何结构与任务空间复杂性边界；将源策略选择建模为集合覆盖问题，采用贪心算法求解并保证近似性能。

Result: 实验表明，在LQR控制器和深度强化学习控制器场景下，贪心策略选择比均匀或随机策略更高效地实现ε-覆盖，所需策略数量显著减少；同时提供了可解释的泛化性能保证与任务空间复杂性分析。

Conclusion: 本文提出的符号发散度量与基于贪心的源策略选择方法，为构建简单但可泛化的控制策略提供了有效的性能导向工具与理论支持，适用于多样化的动态系统场景。

Abstract: Policies must operate across diverse conditions, yet a single policy is often conservative while fully adaptive schemes can be complex. We study zero-shot generalization in contextual dynamical systems and introduce a performance-centric, directional task dissimilarity--the signed divergence--that upper bounds the generalization gap from a source context to a target context. The signed divergence induces $\varepsilon$-tolerance sets that certify when a source policy class generalizes, and it yields a concrete notion of task-space complexity: the minimum number of source contexts needed so that every target context incurs at most $\varepsilon$ generalization gap. Under a mild local smoothness assumption on performance, the induced tolerance sets admit certified inner/outer balls and instance-dependent volume bounds on task-space complexity. In the finite-oracle setting, source selection reduces to set cover; a greedy strategy inherits the standard $H(n)$ approximation guarantee. Using a Mass-Spring-Damper system with linear-quadratic regulator (LQR) controllers and a nonlinear CartPole system with deep reinforcement learning controllers, we show that greedy selection achieves the same $\varepsilon$-coverage with fewer policies than uniform or random baselines. Our approach delivers a performance-based task similarity measure and practical certificates for building generalizable control with simple policies.

</details>

Semi-supervised approaches offer a practical alternative for limited-data settings by using unlabeled observations to reveal latent patterns that experts can interpret. In this paper, we present a semi-supervised RF detection and classification workflow for satellite monitoring that combines Non-negative Matrix Factorization with automatic model determination (NMFk), expert-guided cluster interpretation, and classifier-based prediction. We first represent RF observations as a non-negative feature matrix and apply NMFk to estimate the number of clusters that best captures patterns in the unlabeled data. Subject-matter experts then assign physical meaning to the resulting clusters, including satellite detections, ionospheric environmental conditions, and other RF event categories. Finally, we train a classifier on these interpreted clusters to evaluate performance on a test set and categorize future observations. This pipeline reduces reliance on large pre-labeled datasets by pairing unsupervised factorization with expert interpretation, enabling an interpretable and transferable methodology for detecting, observing, and classifying behavior in RF data.

### [107] [Continuous-Time Probabilistic Correctors for Uncertainty-Aware Physics-Based Spacecraft Trajectory Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21021)

Abstract: Long-horizon spacecraft trajectory forecasting suffers from error accumulation due to the absence of corrective observations in the forecast regime, making reliable uncertainty estimation crucial for safety-critical decision-making such as space domain awareness and conjunction assessment. While high-fidelity physics-based orbit propagators provide accurate deterministic forecasts, they typically lack calibrated uncertainty estimates over long horizons. We introduce a Predictor--Corrector framework in which a physics-based continuous-time $\textit{deterministic}$ forecaster is augmented with a learned continuous-time $\textit{probabilistic}$ Corrector that models forecast errors. The proposed Corrector can be wrapped around an existing deterministic propagator to improve forecast accuracy while producing sharp and calibrated full-covariance uncertainty estimates. The Corrector is based on Latent Neural Controlled Differential Equations (Latent NCDEs) and models the probabilistic temporal evolution of forecast errors in continuous time, naturally supporting irregular sampling and missing features. We further introduce a loss function that promotes calibration and sharpness in long-horizon uncertainty propagation. We evaluate the proposed framework on long-horizon spacecraft trajectory forecasting using real-world data from NASA's Crustal Dynamics Data Information System (CDDIS), wrapping the Corrector around NASA's General Mission Analysis Tool (GMAT). Across forecast horizons of 2--4 days without observations and six rolling test windows, the proposed approach consistently improves accuracy and uncertainty calibration compared to deterministic baselines and Latent ODE-based correctors, demonstrating the effectiveness of the continuous-time probabilistic Corrector for trajectory forecasting.

### [109] [Demystifying Numerical Instability in LLM Inference: Achieving Reproducible Inference for Mission-Critical Tasks with HEAL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21023)
*Zhenting Zhu,Lucas Thai,Shan Yu,Yicheng Liu,Yifan Qiao,Chenxi Wang,Harry Xu,Junyi Shu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出HEAL（Hybrid Error ALleviation）方法，解决大语言模型在异构GPU上因16位精度下采样导致的输出不可重现问题。通过INT16量化和代数误差补偿策略，在不增加内存开销的前提下实现接近FP32的数值稳定性，显著提升计算效率。实验表明，HEAL在保持与FP32基线相同可重现性的同时，性能开销降低最多达7.1倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在金融、医疗、法律等关键领域部署大语言模型时，输出可重现性成为严格系统要求。尽管使用贪婪解码消除算法随机性，但在16位精度下仍存在因硬件异构导致的灾难性输出差异，主要由内核边界处的截断误差引起。

Method: 提出HEAL方法，包含两个核心机制：(1) 对Q、K、V张量采用INT16量化，利用浮点格式未充分利用的位宽，维持数值稳定性且不增加KV缓存开销；(2) 通过代数误差补偿策略，在16位张量核心上合成高精度矩阵乘法，实现近似FP32精度。

Result: 在自建的MCR-Bench基准测试中，HEAL实现了与FP32基线相同的输出可重现性，同时将性能开销降低最多达7.1倍，有效平衡了精度与效率。

Conclusion: HEAL成功解决了16位精度下大语言模型输出不可重现的问题，通过轻量级、硬件友好的设计，在不牺牲可重现性的前提下大幅提升了系统效率，为关键任务场景下的模型部署提供了实用方案。

Abstract: As Large Language Models (LLMs) deploy into mission-critical domains (e.g., finance, medicine, and law), output reproducibility has become a strict system requirement. While practitioners use greedy decoding to eliminate algorithmic stochasticity, empirical deployments with 16-bit precisions still exhibit catastrophic output divergence across heterogeneous GPUs. Through SASS-level profiling, we reveal that this inconsistency is fundamentally driven by truncation errors introduced during downcasting at kernel boundaries. However, achieving reproducibility via a global FP32 pipeline incurs prohibitive system penalties: bypassing 16-bit hardware accelerators hurts compute efficiency, while upcasting the KV cache doubles memory overhead. To bridge this gap, we propose Hybrid Error ALleviation (HEAL), a targeted intervention that approximates FP32 precision while resolving hardware constraints through two targeted mechanisms. First, recognizing that floating-point formats underutilize their bit-width for Q, K, V tensors, HEAL applies INT16 quantization that preserves numerical stability without expanding the KV cache footprint. Second, HEAL synthesizes high-precision matrix multiplications via an algebraic error compensation strategy, executing entirely on high-throughput 16-bit Tensor Cores. To evaluate our approach practically, we introduce MCR-Bench, a benchmark targeting reproducibility in mission-critical tasks. HEAL achieves the same level of reproducibility on downstream tasks as the FP32 baseline while reducing the performance overhead by up to 7.1x.

### [110] [An Efficient and Effective Architecture for Large-Scale Traffic Prediction via Geometry-Adaptive Square Partitioning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21072)

Despite the effectiveness of mainstream neural-network based methods, their deployment in real-world settings with thousands of traffic sensors is jeopardized severely by their poor computational scalability. To address this, the community has attempted to incorporate spatial database partitioning techniques (e.g., Grid, Quadtree, and K-D Tree) to improve model scalability. However, these approaches rely on handcrafted geometric heuristics and often produce irregular or imbalanced data partitions, leading to boundary fragmentation, excessive padding overheads, and degraded model accuracy. In this paper, we propose SqLinear, an efficient and effective architecture for large-scale traffic prediction. First, we design Square Partition, a geometry-adaptive algorithm that partitions massive traffic sensors into balanced, non-overlapping, and near-square spatial regions. Unlike existing heuristic-based designs, Square Partition is theoretically grounded and provides provable guarantees on aspect ratio, balance, and partition utilization, establishing a high-quality foundation for downstream spatiotemporal modeling. Next, we propose a Hierarchical Linear Interaction (HLI) module that abandons the costly attention mechanisms commonly used in Transformer-based spatio-temporal models. HLI efficiently captures both local intra-region dynamics and global inter-region dependencies through a lightweight linear interaction scheme, enabling effective spatiotemporal modeling with linear computational complexity. Extensive experiments on four large-scale traffic datasets and 10 baselines show that SqLinear reduces MAE by 2.30% on average under standard setting and by 5.81% under extreme scalability settings, while reducing training runtime by 13.27%--30.84% in spatial- and horizon-scaling scenarios.

Abstract: Offline-to-online adaptation serves as a pivotal paradigm for mitigating the prohibitive cost of online exploration by bootstrapping reinforcement learning from offline datasets. While this paradigm has been extensively studied in single-agent settings, its extension to Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (MARL) remains largely unexplored, despite its critical relevance to complex coordinated decision-making. To bridge this gap, we introduce Sim2O, an elegant and minimalist framework for offline-to-online MARL. Rather than treating adaptation as a monolithic joint decision, Sim2O conceptualizes it as a compositional process. Specifically, candidate joint actions are synthesized by dynamically blending offline and online action proposals across agents. By leveraging a centralized value function to evaluate these hybrid combinations, Sim2O identifies high-value coordination strategies without requiring auxiliary training objectives or structural overhead. Empirical evaluations across diverse benchmarks demonstrate that Sim2O significantly outperforms existing baselines, underscoring that a minimalist design is not only viable but highly effective for multi-agent offline-to-online adaptation.

</details>

It provides a graphical interface that enables users to input their experimental parameters, optimization objectives, and legacy data. This is then used to build surrogate models, which are coupled with acquisition functions to guide and optimize a process towards a desired objective. To facilitate model building, BASIL provides a variety of predefined surrogate model templates. BASIL can be used to optimize any arbitrary experiment or process with known, user-defined input variables, optimization objectives, and defined output.

### [113] [SLeDGe: Semi-Supervised Learning on Data Streams with Graph Structure Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21096)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出SLeDGe方法，联合学习预测模型与自适应图结构；采用差异化更新策略维护有标签和无标签记忆；通过引入图结构稀疏性约束，抑制噪声连接，增强标签传播效果。

Conclusion: SLeDGe 通过动态建模样本关系与高效记忆管理，在资源受限的数据流环境中实现了卓越的半监督学习性能，为动态数据场景下的标签利用提供了新范式。

Abstract: Semi-supervised learning (SSL) on data streams is challenging due to the continuous evolution of high-volume data and the scarcity of labels. Existing methods are limited in leveraging the intrinsic relationships among samples because they typically rely on fixed similarity measures or static graph structures, which cannot capture how relationships evolve over time. We propose SLeDGe, an SSL method for data streams that jointly learns a predictive model and an adaptive graph structure under strict memory and label constraints. SLeDGe maintains compact labeled and unlabeled memories using distinct update strategies, balancing rapid adaptation to novel features with the retention of historical consistency. In addition, by encouraging sparsity in the relational graph, SLeDGe filters out spurious connections and enables effective propagation of label supervision. Across 12 datasets, SLeDGe outperforms state-of-the-art competitors, achieving average relative accuracy gains of 31.7% with 0.1% labels and 14.8% with 1% labels.

### [115] [Chem2Gen-Bench: Benchmarking Chemical-to-Genetic Translation in Perturbation Response Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21109)
*Yuxiang Lin,Ying Chen*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多单独评估化学或遗传扰动的响应预测，缺乏对化学到遗传扰动跨模态转换的系统性测试。因此亟需一个统一的基准来评估两者在相同靶点背景下的可互换性与对齐能力。

Abstract: Virtual-cell and perturbation models are increasingly used to predict cellular responses for biomedical discovery, but chemical and genetic perturbations are not automatically interchangeable. We introduce Chem2Gen-Bench, a benchmark comprising 260,084 chemical and 1,099,045 genetic perturbation profiles organized into cell-target contexts, and evaluate pairwise alignment, retrieval, protocol covariate associations, feature spaces, and foundation-model embeddings. Across matched contexts, translation fidelity is measurable but heterogeneous; background adjustment increases the association between pairwise similarity and retrieval success, while paired tests show lower mean retrieval success after adjustment under the evaluated settings. In a target-matched K562 audit, the evaluated foundation-model embeddings did not consistently improve over gene-delta baselines. Chem2Gen-Bench provides an auditable framework for testing when chemical and genetic perturbations align around shared targets and when representation gains are supported by matched perturbation evidence.

### [116] [What Accuracy and Gradient Cosine Miss: Evaluating Feedback Alignment via Scale Stability, Reference Validity, and Depth Utility](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21126)
*Yuren Hao,Xiang Wan,ChengXiang Zhai*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文指出当前反馈对齐（FA）方法评估中依赖的任务准确率和余弦相似度的报告方式存在缺陷，因无法检测两种隐蔽的失败模式：测量退化（任务精度下降时梯度参考值坍缩至数值下限）与聚合坍塌（层间异质性被掩盖，信用分配集中在网络一端）。为此，作者提出基于三重检查（尺度稳定性、参考有效性、深度效用）及逐层余弦报告的新诊断评估协议。该协议在多种架构和方法中成功识别所有故障，而传统方法则完全无预警；且两种失败模式具有因果独立性，表明需分别应对。研究揭示了非功能性信用分配的隐患，为开发真正有效的FA方法提供指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有反馈对齐（FA）方法虽在硬件效率与生物合理性上优于反向传播，但其有效性评估依赖于任务准确率与余弦相似度，该标准在某些深层残差网络中会失效，导致错误的正面评价。因此亟需更可靠的评估机制以避免研究人员基于有缺陷的信号构建无效方法。

Method: 提出新的诊断评估协议，包含三项核心检查：1）尺度稳定性（检测残差尺度爆炸引发的参考梯度坍缩）；2）参考有效性（验证反向传播梯度作为参考的合理性）；3）深度效用（评估各层信用分配的实际贡献）。同时改用逐层而非整体平均的余弦相似度报告，以暴露层间异质性。

Result: 在多个深度网络架构（如带有层归一化的残差结构）中，传统评估指标均未发现任何异常，而新协议成功识别出所有已知故障，且具备宽泛的校准裕度。实验表明，通过局部块尺度惩罚可缓解第一类失败（测量退化），但不影响第二类失败（信用分配排名与功能指标矛盾），证明两类失败机制独立。

Conclusion: 当前主流评估范式存在严重盲区，可能误导研究方向。新提出的诊断协议能有效揭露隐藏的信用分配失败，确保后续方法建立在真实有效的学习信号基础上，推动更可靠反馈对齐技术的发展。

Abstract: Despite the success of deep learning, training deep networks in biologically plausible and hardware-efficient ways remains an open challenge. Feedback alignment (FA) methods address this by replacing backpropagation's symmetric backward weights with fixed random matrices, but their effectiveness depends critically on whether they can be accurately evaluated. The standard evaluation relies on two quantities: task accuracy and cosine similarity between the method's credit signal and the backpropagation gradient. We show that this reporting pair is insufficient by identifying two independent failure modes, both silent under current reporting: (1) measurement degeneracy, where the BP reference gradient collapses to the numerical floor in terminal-LayerNorm residual architectures, rendering cosine uninterpretable; and (2) aggregation collapse, where the aggregate cosine masks layerwise heterogeneity that concentrates credit at one end of the network. To address these limitations, we propose a diagnostic evaluation protocol based on three checks -- scale stability, reference validity, and depth utility -- together with per-layer rather than aggregate cosine reporting. Across multiple architectures and methods, the standard reporting pair gives no signal of failure in any audited case, while our protocol identifies all failures with wide calibration margins. The two failure modes are causally independent: a per-block scale penalty alleviates Mode 1 (residual scale explosion driving reference collapse) without affecting Mode 2 (cosine ranking that contradicts every functional metric we measured). Identifying these silent failures prevents researchers from building on non-functional credit assignment and provides actionable guidance for developing FA methods that genuinely train deep layers.

</details>


### [117] [Horizon Adaptive Offline Policy Learning via Value Stitching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21136)
*Kexin Zheng,Xianyuan Zhan,Xintao Yan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: VAST提出一种基于动态时间跨度的值函数学习方法，通过递归自适应的值组合机制，替代传统固定步长的TD学习，实现更灵活、准确的值估计。该方法利用条件辅助值函数与拼接策略，实现可行动子目标状态下的变长回报直接估计与组合，显著提升复杂长时任务中的离线策略学习性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统TD学习存在值估计偏差累积问题，而现有扩展时域方法采用固定时域策略，难以适应复杂长时任务中的多阶段价值结构。需要一种更具灵活性的动态时域建模方法来提高值函数准确性。

Method: 提出Horizon Adaptive Offline Policy Learning via VAlue STitching (VAST)，通过引入未来状态和时域长度条件化的辅助值函数，并结合最优时域选择的拼接策略，实现递归、自适应的值函数组合。该方法支持基于可行动子目标的变长回报直接估计与拼接，提供精准且可贪婪利用的值监督信号。

Abstract: Learning accurate value functions plays a decisive role for reinforcement learning (RL) agents to solve long-horizon, complex tasks. Conventional temporal-difference (TD) learning objectives suffer from value-estimation bias that accumulates over the horizon, while extended-horizon modeling methods, such as n-step TD backups and Q-chunking, adopt a rigid, fixed-horizon value-modeling recipe that is often not flexible enough to capture complex value structures in long-horizon, multi-stage tasks. In this paper, we show that enabling value updates with dynamic horizon composition can yield a strong offline policy learning scheme. Our method, Horizon Adaptive Offline Policy Learning via VAlue STitching (VAST), replaces fixed-horizon backups with recursive, horizon-adaptive value composition. Its key ingredient is to couple value optimization with a future state- and horizon-length-conditioned auxiliary value function that is learned through direct data supervision, and a stitching policy that optimally selects the reward-maximizing horizon length and future sub-goal to achieve horizon-adaptive value stitching. This design enables direct estimation and compositional "stitching" of variable-length returns grounded in actionable sub-goal states, providing an accurate and greedily exploitable value-supervision signal for offline policy optimization. Across 50 tasks on OGBench, VAST outperforms fixed-step, extended-horizon methods, and generative-value offline RL baselines, achieving strong performance particularly in high-complexity, long-horizon decision-making tasks.

### [118] [Dead-Direction Signatures: A Cheap Spectral Reading of Singular Complexity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21158)
*Tejas Pradeep Shirodkar,P. J. Narayanan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为死方向签名（DDS）的新方法，通过网络激活矩阵或样本梯度Fisher-Gram的谱分析，以闭式解析方式快速估计深度网络损失奇异性的几何结构。该方法基于死方向框架和秩乘体积恒等式，能够从谱中直接读取死方向数量（秩缺陷 $r$），且无需像SGLD那样进行大量前向-反向传播。在低秩回归和非线性模块加法Transformer上，DDS表现优异，能精确追踪真实学习系数（RLCT），而传统校准后的局部学习系数（LLC）在预算限制下则呈现平直结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法如SGLD需要大量计算资源和任务特定校准，难以高效评估深层网络复杂性；亟需一种低成本、可解析计算的替代方案来捕捉损失函数奇异点的几何特征。

Method: 引入死方向签名（DDS），利用激活矩阵与梯度Fisher-Gram的谱特性，构建基于秩乘体积恒等式的闭式谱读数，通过最小特征值的秩盲性质识别死方向数量，并实现对网络秩缺陷的精确跟踪。

Result: 在低秩回归任务中，校准后的LLC恢复了真实RLCT达99%准确率；而DDS不仅实现了对真实$\lambda$的精确追踪，还在18个数量级的模块化Transformer中成功分离出模型维度 $d_{\mathrm{model}}$，表现出远超传统LLC的灵敏度与效率。

Conclusion: DDS提供了一种廉价、闭式、层局部的网络奇异结构分析工具，补充了基于积分后验的LLC方法，为理解深度网络复杂性提供了新的方向性视角。

Abstract: Singular learning theory characterises the complexity of a deep network through the geometry of its loss singularities. The local learning coefficient (LLC), the standard estimator of Watanabe's real log canonical threshold (RLCT, $λ$), reads this geometry as an integrated Bayesian scalar through SGLD, which needs per-task calibration and $10^4$-$10^6$ forward-backward passes per checkpoint. We introduce Dead-Direction Signatures (DDS), a family of cheap closed-form spectral readings of singular structure: each reads a network's activation matrix or per-sample-gradient Fisher-Gram at a chosen layer, replacing the SGLD posterior chain with spectral linear algebra. The readings rest on a dead-direction framework that predicts a structural correlation between activation- and Fisher-side spectra at any singular minimum, and a rank-multiplicative volume identity that single-eigenvalue monitors cannot produce: the active-volume $\log\det^{+}(G)$ slope counts the dead directions, tracking the rank-deficit $r$ across $r \in \{1,2,3,4\}$ (slope ratios $2.0, 3.1, 4.0$ at $r{=}2,3,4$ against the predicted $2,3,4$), where the smallest eigenvalue is rank-blind. On reduced-rank regression with closed-form $λ$, calibrated LLC recovers $λ$ at $99\%$ mean and the DDS observables rank-track it at the framework-predicted sign; on a non-linear modular-addition transformer DDS separates $d_{\mathrm{model}}$ across eighteen orders of magnitude where calibrated LLC at the protocol budget is rank-flat. Complementary to LLC's integrated posterior reading, DDS gives a directional, layer-local handle on a network's dead directions, read in closed form from its activation and gradient spectra.

</details>

### [120] [Beyond Fixed Budgets: Characterizing the Inelasticity and Limitations of Tree-of-Thought Reasoning Strategies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20599)
*Atkia Mahila,Avinash Maurya,M. Mustafa Rafique,Bogdan Nicolae*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究系统评估了两种典型的思维树（ToT）搜索方法（DPTS和SSDP）在不同计算预算、模型规模和问题难度下的表现。结果显示，DPTS在低预算下存在冷启动瓶颈，需大量探索才能获得可靠价值估计，不适合资源受限场景；而SSDP虽能快速生成候选解，但因激进的节点合并导致路径枯竭，无法随预算增加持续改进。两者分别暴露了固定探索与固定剪枝策略的局限性，表明科学推理代理需要能根据搜索进展和资源动态调整行为的自适应策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前对思维树（ToT）搜索方法在实际部署中的表现缺乏系统性研究，尤其在不同计算预算、模型规模和问题难度下的行为差异尚不明确。本文旨在揭示现有方法的局限性，并为构建更高效的自适应搜索策略提供依据。

Method: 在Math500和GSM8K两个数学推理基准上，对比评估DPTS（基于蒙特卡洛树搜索）和SSDP（基于语义去重）两种方法，覆盖Llama-3B和Llama-8B两种模型规模，以及3k–10k token四种预算设置，通过多维度实验分析其性能表现与瓶颈。

Result: DPTS在低预算下表现差，因冷启动问题导致价值估计不可靠，但在高预算下表现出良好扩展性；SSDP能快速生成解，但因过度合并节点导致未探索路径永久丢失，难以进一步优化。两者均无法在全计算范围内保持高效，凸显固定策略的不足。

Conclusion: 单一固定的探索或剪枝策略无法适应不同的计算资源条件。未来有效的科学推理搜索应具备根据搜索进度和可用资源动态调整行为的能力，强调自适应策略的重要性。

Abstract: Tree of Thought (ToT) search has become a promising direction for improving the reasoning capabilities of large language models, but deploying these methods in practice raises a question that has received little systematic attention: how do different search strategies behave under varying compute budgets, model sizes, and problem difficulties? In this work, we evaluate two representative ToT methods; DPTS, a Monte Carlo tree search based approach, and SSDP, a semantic deduplication based approach, across two mathematical reasoning benchmarks (Math500 and GSM8K), two model scales (Llama-3B and Llama-8B), and four token budgets (3k--10k). Our analysis reveals that the two methods exhibit limitations that pull in opposite directions. DPTS suffers from a cold-start bottleneck at low budgets: it requires sufficient exploration before its value estimates become reliable, making it a poor fit for resource-constrained settings despite strong scaling behavior at higher budgets. SSDP, on the other hand, reaches candidate solutions efficiently but is prone to frontier depletion; its aggressive node merging permanently discards unexplored paths, leaving it unable to improve regardless of how much budget remains. Together, these findings suggest that neither a fixed exploration strategy nor a fixed pruning strategy is sufficient across compute continuum. We argue that effective search for scientific reasoning agents requires strategies that can adapt their behavior based on search progress and available resources.

</details>


### [121] [The New Associationism: Lessons from Deep Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20600)
*Daniel Rothschild*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文探讨现代人工智能的成功对人类学习的启示，认为将AI视为人类学习的模型支持一种温和但真实的联结主义观点。核心发现是监督学习（由评价性反馈驱动的学习）贯穿于当代多种AI系统，从大语言模型到游戏博弈代理，主要差异在于生成反馈信号所需的工作量。这证实了联结主义关于统一、渐进、错误驱动学习机制跨领域运作的理想，并化解了过去认为联结主义机制不足以解释人类认知能力的争议。然而，深度学习的成功依赖于远超古典联结主义设想的计算架构，且监督学习仅作为其中一环，而非学习的完整解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究现代人工智能的成功是否能为理解人类学习提供新视角，特别是检验联结主义理论在解释复杂认知能力方面的有效性。

Method: 通过分析当前主流人工智能系统（如大语言模型和游戏博弈代理）中监督学习的作用，比较其反馈生成机制的差异，结合历史联结主义理论进行对比论证。

Result: 监督学习在多种先进AI系统中普遍存在，且其运作模式与联结主义理想高度契合；但深度学习架构超越了传统联结主义框架，表明监督学习只是整体学习机制的一部分。

Conclusion: 现代AI的成功为联结主义提供了新的支持，但同时也揭示其局限性——必须结合更复杂的计算架构才能实现真正的人类水平智能。

Abstract: What can the success of modern AI tell us about how humans learn? This paper argues that taking AI seriously as a model of human learning supports a modest but genuine associationism. The central finding is that supervised learning -- learning driven by evaluative feedback -- underlies a surprisingly wide range of contemporary AI systems, from large language models to game-playing agents, differing primarily in how much work is required to generate the relevant feedback signal. This vindicates associationist ideals of a uniform, gradual, error-driven learning mechanism operating across domains, and defuses the once-influential argument that associationist mechanisms are too limited to account for human cognitive capacities. At the same time, the successes of deep learning depend on computational architectures that go well beyond anything classical associationists envisaged, and supervised learning operates within these as one component rather than a complete account of learning.

</details>


### [122] [Specifying AI-SDLC Processes: A Protocol Language for Human-Agent Boundaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20615)
*Ylli Prifti*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种领域特定语言（DSL），用于规范人工智能在软件开发生命周期（AI-SDLC）中的协作过程，明确人类与AI的责任边界、审批节点和治理约束。该语言具备形式化语法、良构性条件、操作语义及执行不变量，区分策略（意图）与机制（结构化强制），通过验证令牌和能力边界等原语控制过程的非确定性。三个核心成果包括：失败率分析表明结构化强制可将系统失败率限制为代理与验证者速率的加权乘积；2+N团队模式形式化了AI-SDLC中的职责分离；编排循环的克林闭包与协议自验证成为设计特性而非特例。相比多智能体框架、工作流规范和基于能力的安全模型，本文创新在于这些元素的集成而非单一技术。已实现原型证明可行性，但实证评估仍需未来工作。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI作为软件开发全生命周期中的第一类成员，但缺乏统一的规范语言来表达人机协作中的责任边界、审批机制和治理约束。现有方法要么将流程编码于代理提示中（易漂移），要么聚焦邻近领域（如工作流管理、业务流程），或仅解决局部问题（如访问控制、审批）。因此亟需一种能形式化表达AI-SDLC协作过程的专用语言。

Method: 提出一种领域特定语言（DSL），支持将AI-SDLC过程建模为协议。该语言包含形式化语法、良构性条件、操作语义和执行不变量，强调策略（声明意图）与机制（结构化强制）的分离。利用验证令牌、能力边界等原语控制过程非确定性，并通过形式化分析验证其可靠性。

Result: 1. 失败率分析显示，结构化强制可将系统失败率控制在代理与验证者失败率的加权乘积水平，而行为合规可能导致累积或接近饱和的增长；2. 提出2+N团队模式，形式化了经典职责分离原则在AI-SDLC中的应用；3. 编排循环的克林闭包与协议自验证被证明是自然的设计属性，而非特殊构造。

Conclusion: 本文提出的DSL通过整合策略与机制、引入结构化强制与形式化保障，为AI-SDLC协作提供了可验证、可扩展的规范基础。其核心贡献在于多种关键要素的有机集成，而非单一技术突破。原型实现验证了可行性，未来工作将开展实证评估。

Abstract: AI agents now participate as first-class team members across the software development lifecycle, yet no specification language exists for expressing the human-agent responsibility boundaries, approval gates, and governance constraints this collaboration requires. Existing approaches encode process in agent prompts (subject to drift), target adjacent domains (workflow management, business processes), or address only fragments (access control, approval gates).
  We propose a domain-specific language for specifying AI-SDLC processes as protocols, with formal syntax, well-formedness conditions, operational semantics, and enforcement invariants. The language distinguishes policy (declared intent) from mechanism (structural enforcement), enabling implementations to bound process non-determinism through primitives such as validation tokens and capability boundaries.
  Three results follow. A failure rate analysis shows that structural enforcement bounds system failure rates at a weighted product of agent and validator rates, while behavioral compliance permits cumulative or near-saturating growth. The 2+N team pattern (two human-in-control roles plus N specialized agent members) formalizes classical Separation of Duties for AI-SDLC. Kleene closure of orchestration loops and reflexive protocol-adherence validation emerge as design properties rather than special-case constructs.
  We position the contribution against multi-agent frameworks (MetaGPT), workflow specification (FlowAgent, BPMN extensions), and capability-based security (SAGA): the novelty lies in the specific integration, not any single primitive. A working implementation demonstrates feasibility; empirical evaluation is future work.

### [123] [PEAR: Permutation-Equivariant Adaptive Routing Multi-Agent Debate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20621)
*Yang Feng,Ziwei Xu,Xia Hu,Fengxiang He*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: PEAR提出一种动态可配置的多智能体辩论协议，通过在推理阶段重新分配通信角色和稀疏拓扑结构，解决固定拓扑带来的位置偏差和角色敏感性问题。该方法利用代理状态自适应调整角色分配，确保无代理长期占据优势地位，提升整体可靠性与公平性。理论分析表明其具有等变性与稀疏路由特性，实证结果在四个推理基准和六种LLM架构上均显著优于现有最强基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于多智能体辩论的方法受限于固定拓扑结构，易产生持久的位置偏差、放大不可靠代理的影响，并对角色分配高度敏感。为提升大语言模型推理的可靠性与鲁棒性，亟需一种能够动态调节通信结构与角色分配的机制。

Method: 提出Permutation-Equivariant Adaptive Routing Multi-Agent Debate (PEAR)，在推理阶段动态重配置代理间的通信角色与稀疏拓扑；通过根据代理状态变化调整角色分配，实现网络位置的均衡分布与影响扩散，具备等变性与低复杂度路由特性。

Result: 在四个推理任务基准和六种不同大语言模型架构上的实验表明，PEAR显著提升了平均准确率，优于当前最强的辩论基线方法。

Conclusion: PEAR通过动态角色与拓扑重配置，有效缓解了多智能体辩论中的位置偏差与角色依赖问题，增强了模型推理的稳定性与泛化能力，是一种高效且鲁棒的推理优化框架。

Abstract: Multi-agent debate improves the reliability of large language models (LLMs) through iterative peer critiques. However, fixed topologies often introduce persistent positional biases, amplify unreliable agents, and cause high sensitivity to role assignments. We introduce \textit{Permutation-Equivariant Adaptive Routing Multi-Agent Debate (PEAR)}, an inference-time protocol that dynamically reconfigures communication roles and sparse topologies across consecutive debate rounds. By strategically switching agent-to-role assignments based on evolving agent states, PEAR prevents any agent from permanently occupying a privileged network position or distributes influence more evenly across the debate. We theoretically characterize PEAR as an equivariant sparse router: it preserves accuracy under agent relabeling while reducing routing complexity and improving generalization. Comprehensive empirical evaluations across four reasoning benchmarks and six diverse LLM backbones demonstrate PEAR significantly improves average accuracy over the strongest debate baselines. The code is at https://github.com/EVIEHub/PEAR.

Method: 采用移动图形用户界面（GUI）作为复杂世界代理；构建Darwin Mobile Agent开源框架，通过异步代理-环境循环在多个云手机实例上并行执行任务，减少数据收集瓶颈；提出从任务课程、结果验证到记忆管理三个核心支柱逐步消除人类先验的路线图。

Conclusion: 本研究为迈向真正自主、自演化的人工智能系统建立了理论与实践基础，展示了通过复杂环境交互实现智能自然演化的可行性。

Abstract: The goal of artificial intelligence is to create agents capable of general, adaptive behaviour in open-ended environments. Guided by the "Bitter Lesson", we argue that the most effective path toward this goal is to systematically remove human priors and allow intelligence to naturally emerge through interaction with a "Big World" that is orders of magnitude more complex than the agent itself. We propose the mobile Graphical User Interface (GUI) as a practical proxy for such a world and introduce Darwin Mobile Agent, an open-source infrastructure designed as a foundation for autonomous reinforcement learning in this domain. This framework addresses the data-collection bottleneck in real-world mobile interactions by using an asynchronous agent-environment loop across parallel cloud-phone instances. We further propose a conceptual roadmap to systematically remove human priors from three fundamental pillars of a self-evolving agent: task curricula, outcome verification, and memory management. We validate that the Darwin infrastructure provides the stability and scalability required for the first stage of this roadmap: policy optimisation in the GUI domain. This work establishes the practical and theoretical foundation necessary to move toward truly autonomous, self-evolving GUI agents.

### [125] [Path-dependent program induction under resource constraints explains human sequence learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20623)
*Hanqi Zhou,David G. Nagy,Peter Dayan,Charley M. Wu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了在认知资源有限的情况下，人们如何从序列经验中构建抽象且可重用的知识。通过将速率-失真理论与程序归纳进展结合，提出一种分层适配语法（HAG），包含局部（任务内）和全局（跨任务）知识库，受记忆和计算约束共同调控。模拟结果显示，HAG在速率-失真权衡和泛化能力上优于固定语法或浅层分块方法。在线旋律序列学习实验中，参与者回忆错误表现出系统性简化，反应时在推断出的程序边界处增加。逐次试验拟合表明，分层知识库能最好地解释个体在回忆和样本外延续选择中的差异，优于所有替代模型。研究揭示结构化学习本质上是受约束的程序归纳，经验顺序塑造学习者未来形成的抽象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究人类在有限认知资源下如何从序列经验中构建抽象、可复用的知识，理解先验知识如何影响未来结构的编码成本与发现难度。

Method: 结合速率-失真理论与程序归纳，提出分层适配语法（HAG），包含局部与全局知识库，通过记忆与计算约束进行联合调控；采用模拟与在线实验验证模型性能及人类行为匹配度。

Result: HAG在模拟中表现更优，具有更好的速率-失真权衡与更强泛化能力；实验中参与者回忆误差呈现系统性简化，反应时在程序边界上升高；分层知识库模型最能解释个体差异，优于其他模型。

Conclusion: 结构化学习可被理解为受约束的程序归纳过程，经验的顺序决定了学习者未来构建抽象的方式，先验知识通过影响程序的可编码性与可发现性塑造认知发展。

Abstract: How do people build abstract, reusable knowledge from sequential experience under bounded cognitive resources? To answer this question, we integrate rate-distortion theory with recent advances in program induction to describe how prior knowledge shapes which future structures are cheap to encode and easy to discover. We formalize this in a hierarchical Adaptor Grammar (HAG) with distinct local (within-task) and global (across-task) libraries, governed jointly by constraints on memory and computation. In simulations, HAG achieves better rate-distortion trade-offs and stronger generalization than fixed grammars or shallow chunking methods. In an online melodic sequence-learning experiment, participants' recall errors reflected systematic simplifications and reaction times increased at inferred program boundaries. Trial-by-trial fits further showed that hierarchical libraries best explained individual differences in both recall and out-of-sample continuation choices, outperforming all alternative models. These findings cast structured learning as bounded program induction in which the order of experience shapes future abstractions a learner builds.

### [126] [In LLM Reasoning, there is Irrationality on top of Value Misalignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20624)
*Kejiang Qian,Fengxiang He*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文提出并形式化了理性价值风险（rational value risk），即模型在推理过程中实际采用的策略与理论上最优（最大化期望效用）策略之间的效用差距。研究发现，即使经过良好对齐的LLM，在推理阶段仍可能无法最大化其对齐的价值函数。通过分解估计误差为有限候选、有限提示和不完美验证器三部分，作者在多个大模型（如Llama-3.1、Qwen-2.5、T{"}ulu-3、GPT-5.2/5.5、DeepSeek-V4）和基准测试（UltraFeedback、AlpacaEval、GSM8K、MATH、HumanEval、MathArena）上进行了广泛实验，验证了：(1) 理性价值风险普遍存在；(2) 价值对齐可降低但无法消除该风险；(3) 风险高度依赖推理策略；(4) 更长推理能提升理性度，但收益递减。代码已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大语言模型在训练阶段已被良好对齐于目标价值函数，但在实际推理过程中，其决策策略可能仍偏离理论上的最优（最大化期望效用）路径，导致效用损失。这种‘对齐’与‘理性执行’之间的差距亟需被识别和量化，以推动更可靠、更理性的生成行为。

Method: 提出理性价值风险的数学定义，将其视为部署时推理策略与理想理性策略之间的效用差；通过分解估计误差来源（有限候选、有限提示、不完美验证器）来分析影响因素；设计多模型、多任务实验框架，系统评估不同模型和推理策略下的风险表现。

Result: (1) 理性价值风险在多种模型和任务中普遍存在；(2) 价值对齐虽能缓解风险，但无法根除；(3) 推理策略显著影响风险大小；(4) 延长推理过程可逐步提升理性水平，但存在边际递减效应。

Conclusion: 当前的大语言模型即便在训练中实现良好对齐，其推理行为仍面临显著的理性价值风险。这表明，仅靠训练阶段对齐不足以保证推理中的最优决策，需在推理阶段引入更精细的控制机制，如基于验证器的反馈或自洽性优化，以逼近理性策略。

Abstract: Significant progress has been made in aligning LLMs with target value functions. We argue that, even when an LLM has been well aligned in (post-)training, it may still fail to maximise the aligned value in reasoning. We mathematically formalise this gap as rational value risk: the utility discrepancy between a model's deployed reasoning strategy and its rational counterpart, which is defined to be the responses that maximise expected utility in the steepest direction. The estimation error of rational value risk is further decomposed into three components from finite candidates, finite prompts, and imperfect verifiers. Extensive experiments are conducted, covering models Llama-3.1, Qwen-2.5, T{\"}ulu-3 families (7B-72B), GPT-5.2, GPT-5.5, and DeepSeek-V4, and benchmarks UltraFeedback, AlpacaEval, GSM8K, MATH, HumanEval, and MathArena. The results validate that (1) rational value risk is widespread; (2) value alignment can reduce, but cannot eliminate, it; (3) the risk is highly sensitive to inference-time reasoning strategy; and (4) longer reasoning improves rationality with diminishing returns. The code is at https://github.com/EVIEHub/LLM-Rationality.

</details>


### [127] [AlphaMemo: Structured Search-Process Memory for Self-Evolving Alpha Mining Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20625)
*Hang Yu,Zifan Zheng,Jeff Z. Pan,Tongliang Liu,Zhiyong Wang,Fengxiang He*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: AlphaMemo 是一种自进化阿尔法挖掘代理，通过结构化搜索-过程记忆解决大模型代理在因子挖掘中的组合爆炸、反馈噪声、冗余发现和过拟合问题。它通过提取抽象语法树（AST）差异中的编辑模式，结合置信度门控残差记忆与搜索账本先验，并使用非对称否决控制抑制高置信度失败模式，显著提升 CSI 500 和 S&P 500 上的样本外表现与固定预算下的发现效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 LLM 代理在金融因子挖掘中面临组合搜索空间大、反馈噪声强且非平稳、重复发现以及因盲目复用历史成功而引发的过拟合风险。需要更智能的记忆机制来支持高效、稳定的因子探索。

Method: 提出 AlphaMemo，引入结构化搜索-过程记忆；记录编辑模式在特定父因子上下文中的有效性；基于 AST 差异提取可复用的编辑动机；采用置信度门控的残差记忆机制；结合搜索账本先验；使用非对称否决控制抑制已知失败模式。

Result: 在 CSI 500 与 S&P 500 数据集上均实现更好的样本外表现和固定预算下的因子发现效率；消融实验验证了残差学习、置信度门控、AST 差异模式及否决记忆的关键作用。

Conclusion: AlphaMemo 通过结构化记忆机制有效缓解了 LLM 代理在因子挖掘中的核心挑战，为自动化、可演化金融因子发现提供了新范式。

Abstract: LLM agents are promising for alpha mining via combining financial priors, symbolic reasoning, executable factor generation, and feedback-driven refinement. Yet, they face a combinatorial search space, noisy non-stationary feedback, redundant discoveries, and overfitting risks from naively reusing past successes. To address these challenges, we propose AlphaMemo, a self-evolving alpha mining agent with Structured Search-Process Memory. Rather than memorizing only final factors or full trajectories, AlphaMemo records reusable evidence about which edit motifs work or fail under specific parent-factor contexts. It extracts motifs from Abstract Syntax Tree (AST) differences, applies confidence-gated residual memory on top of a search-ledger prior, and uses asymmetric veto control to suppress high-confidence failure patterns. Experiments on CSI 500 and S\&P 500 show improved out-of-sample performance and fixed-budget discovery efficiency, with ablations validating the roles of residual learning, confidence gating, AST-diff motifs, and veto memory. Code is at https://github.com/jarrettyu/AlphaMemo.

</details>


### [128] [Latent Goal Prediction from Language for Model-Based Planning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20627)
*Samuel Barbeau,Simon Roy,Giovanni Beltrame,Christian Desrosiers,Nicolas Thome*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: LAGO 是一种从语言指令中预测中间目标状态和动作条件滚动的框架，通过在统一潜在空间中动态分解任务为可处理的子目标，实现长时程、高精度的基于语言的规划。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决世界模型规划中的预测误差累积和难以定义优化目标的问题，特别是视觉目标提供局部梯度但缺乏远距离指导，而语言虽灵活却受限于跨模态对齐噪声或依赖大型生成模型，不适合高采样率的模型基础规划。

Method: 引入潜空间中的语言引导子目标预测（LAGO），将语言指令分解为一系列潜在空间中的中间目标，并结合动作条件滚动，在线更新子目标，使用软最小轨迹成本进行规划，实现长程一致性潜轨迹。

Result: 在多个环境和规划时长下，LAGO 避免了先前方法的性能急剧下降，实现了仅基于语言的鲁棒且精确的长时程规划，兼具视觉目标的精度与语言控制的灵活性。

Conclusion: LAGO 有效融合了语言的灵活性与视觉目标的精确性，为长时程、高复杂度的任务规划提供了新范式。

Abstract: Planning with world models is bottlenecked by compounding prediction errors and the difficulty of defining optimizable goals. Visual targets provide precise local gradients but poor distant guidance, while language is flexible yet limited by noisy cross-modal alignment or dependence on large generative models unsuited for the high-sampling nature of model-based planning. To address these challenges, we introduce Latent Goal Prediction from Language (LAGO), a framework that predicts both sequences of intermediate goal states from language instructions and action-conditioned rollouts, all within the same latent space. Rather than optimizing toward a single global objective, LAGO dynamically decomposes instructions into explicitly predicted, locally tractable latent subgoals. By updating these subgoals online and using a soft minimum trajectory cost during planning, LAGO enables an agent to follow coherent latent trajectories over long horizons. Evaluation across multiple environments planning horizons shows that LAGO avoids the sharp degradation of prior methods. By achieving robust and precise long-horizon planning purely from language, LAGO bridges the precision of visual goals with the flexibility of text-guided control.

### [129] [Human Decision-Making with AI Assistance under Correlated Features](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20628)
*Yanru Guan,Naveen Raman,Fei Fang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 当特征相关时，AI推荐测试需采用先探索后承诺的策略以平衡短期决策质量和长期人类学习；静态推荐策略在特征相关下表现极差，最优策略为动态规划求解，且计算复杂度为NP-hard；近似算法通过短周期规划加静态尾部实现接近最优性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究如何在特征相关情况下，通过AI推荐测试来平衡短期决策质量与长期人类学习，避免静态推荐策略因特征相关导致的性能下降。

Method: 证明特征相关导致静态策略性能恶化，提出探索-承诺结构的最优策略，并基于动态规划设计算法求解有限时间内的最优策略；同时开发一种短周期规划结合静态尾部的近似算法。

Result: 理论证明最优策略必须为探索-承诺结构，且探索阶段长度依赖特征相关程度；计算最优策略为NP-hard；近似算法可实现接近最优性能；实验表明特征相关越强，探索阶段越长。

Conclusion: 在特征相关场景下，AI应先推荐多样化测试以促进人类学习，再固定推荐一组测试；该策略优于静态推荐，且可通过动态规划或近似算法有效实现。

Abstract: Humans increasingly make decisions with AI assistance; for example, doctors may follow AI-recommended diagnostic tests and base their diagnoses on the results. A natural question is which tests should AI recommend to balance short-term decision quality and long-term human learning when different features (e.g., test results) are correlated. While prior work establishes that stationary policies that recommend the same tests repeatedly are optimal when features are independent, we prove that feature correlations lead such policies to perform arbitrarily poorly. Instead, we prove that any optimal policy must follow an explore-then-commit structure; initially, the AI should offer diverse tests so humans can learn accurate feature coefficients, then the AI should commit to a single set of tests, with exploration length that depends on the degree of feature correlation. We prove that computing the optimal policy is NP-hard and derive a dynamic programming-based algorithm that finds the optimal policy for finite horizons. We additionally develop an approximation that plans for shorter horizons and appends a stationary suffix, achieving near-optimal performance. Our empirical results complement our theory by showing that stronger feature correlation leads to longer exploration phases.

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: DEMM-Bench 是一个基于决策证据成熟度模型（DEMM）的跨制度基准，用于评估代理运行时治理证据的充分性。它通过适配器标准化八个证据领域，针对角色、权限、行为、政策、决策依据、资源影响、生命周期上下文和验证强度等属性提出问题，并施加八种确定性退化条件。在64个案例中，有75%的迹线存在和模式存在基线过度自信，50%的账本存在基线过度自信，而经过删减的属性级候选评分器则无过度自信，平均属性充分性准确率为56.25%。该基准提供数据集、构造-真值标签、基线和适配器，支持对异构代理运行时证据底座的可复现评估。

Conclusion: DEMM-Bench 提供了一种可复现的评估框架，能够有效衡量代理运行时治理证据的充分性，揭示现有基线的过度自信问题，并为未来治理系统的设计与验证提供坚实基础。

Abstract: Agent-runtime systems emit traces, ledgers, provenance graphs, policy logs, delegation tokens, cache events, and tool-firewall records, but those containers do not necessarily answer governance questions about a specific decision. DEMM-Bench is a cross-regime benchmark for agent-runtime governance-evidence sufficiency, grounded in the Decision Evidence Maturity Model (DEMM): it measures whether records across eight evidence regimes are sufficient to reconstruct decision-level properties rather than merely present. The benchmark normalizes the regimes through adapters, asks property questions over actor, authority, action, policy, decision basis, resource touch, lifecycle context, and verification strength, and applies eight deterministic degradation conditions. Across 64 manuscript cases, trace-present and schema-present baselines overclaim on 75% of cases, ledger-present overclaims on 50%, and the redacted property-level candidate scorer has zero overclaim with 56.25% mean Property Sufficiency Accuracy. To address this problem, we propose SkillHarness, a framework for safe skill harnessing in dynamic environments. SkillHarness moves beyond static skill abstractions by modeling skill learning and utilization as a safety-constrained interaction process. ### [133] [Constituency Optimisation Through Hamiltonian Representation Of Mandates (COTHROM): Algorithmic Redistricting of Irish Election Boundaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20637)

Abstract: Electoral redistricting in Ireland's Proportional Representation Single Transferable Vote (PR-STV) system faces the challenge of selecting an optimally representative set of electoral boundaries from an enormous set of possible configurations, and where ``representative'' is a delicate balance of constitutional objectives that are often in tension with one another. We present the first computational framework for Irish electoral redistricting that systematically optimises across multiple constitutional requirements while making trade-offs explicit and quantifiable. The electoral redistricting problem is parsed using statistical physics, where constitutional objectives are considered as terms in a Potts Hamiltonian. Markov Chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) methods and simulated annealing are employed to minimise this objective function, systematically exploring this configuration space, with coupling constants as proxies for objective weightings. Multi Criterion Decision Analysis (MCDA) and Pareto Optimality is then utilised to remedy the ambiguity in choosing a certain objective weighting combination over others. With respect to proportional representation and compactness objectives evaluated in County Cork, COTHROM consistently improves on the existing legal constituency boundaries for a range of objective weightings.
