### [134] [RIZZ: Routing Interactions to Near Zero-Interference Zones for Continual Adaptation of Black-Box Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20638)
*Sonali Goel,Pranav Vaidhyanathan,Lucas Schorling,Natalia Ares,Maike Osborne*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: RIZZ 是一种用于复合语言模型系统的持续适应框架，通过验证器门控的记忆、路由和提示编译实现完全黑箱学习。它将输入流动态划分为记忆分支，在推理时根据上下文选择或创建分支，整合局部、全局、图结构和工作记忆的上下文，生成有限提示并结合任务证据。模型执行后，任务验证器评估输出，仅经验证的交互可更新记忆、推广可复用规则、降级有害规则或创建反模式，从而在持续自然语言反馈中提升性能，同时显式控制干扰。该框架针对在线适应且受上下文预算限制的场景，并在竞争性基准测试中优于现有最先进方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有黑箱适应方法在非平稳输入流、稀疏反馈以及跨任务失败污染等问题上表现不佳，难以实现高效持续适应。需要一种能有效管理干扰、支持在线适应并受限于上下文预算的新型框架。

Method: RIZZ 采用验证器门控机制，构建动态记忆分支；利用上下文感知路由器选择或创建分支；整合分支本地、全局、图结构和工作记忆信息；通过提示编译生成受限提示；结合任务验证器对输出评分，仅验证通过的交互可更新记忆或调整规则，实现持续优化。

Result: RIZZ 在多个竞争性基准测试中表现出色，显著优于当前最先进的基线方法，证明其在持续适应、干扰控制和在线学习方面的有效性。

Conclusion: RIZZ 提供了一种高效的黑箱持续适应框架，能够在不访问模型权重的情况下，通过验证器驱动的机制实现稳定、可控且自适应的长期行为演化，适用于多变、复杂的真实应用场景。

Abstract: Large language models are increasingly deployed as long-lived agents that must adapt across users, tasks, domains, modalities, and feedback regimes without access to model weights. Existing black-box adaptation methods typically optimize a single prompt, maintain an undifferentiated memory, or rely on repeated rollout-heavy search. However, these designs struggle when streams of input are nonstationary, feedback is sparse, and failures from one task family can contaminate behavior on another. We introduce RIZZ (Routing Interactions to Near Zero-interference Zones), a continual adaptation framework for compound language-model systems that learns entirely through verifier-gated memory, routing, and prompt compilation. RIZZ organizes input streams into dynamically spawned memory branches. At inference time, either while online or offline, a context-aware router selects or creates a branch that retrieves branch-local, global, graph-structured, and working-memory context, which is compiled into a bounded prompt together with retrieved task evidence. After the model acts, task verifiers score the output, and only verified interactions can update memory, promote reusable rules, demote harmful rules, or create anti-patterns. This yields a black-box agent that improves through persistent natural-language feedback while explicitly controlling interference. RIZZ targets the regime where adaptation must occur online under context budgets. Finally, we demonstrate the effectiveness of our framework against state-of-the-art baselines on competitive benchmarks.

### [135] [An LLM-Explainable DRL Framework for Passenger-Directed Autonomous Driving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20640)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 公众对自动驾驶的信任受限于其决策过程缺乏透明性，因此需要一种既能实现智能驾驶又能向乘客清晰解释行为的系统。

Method: 采用双重双深度Q网络（Dueling Double Deep Q-Network）训练DRL代理以响应不同驾驶请求（如快速、舒适、停止），同时引入大语言模型（LLM）模块来解析乘客意图、判断是否需要解释，并生成基于安全性的简明理由。

Result: DRL代理在仿真中表现出稳定的训练过程、符合交通规则的安全行为以及在单次行程中模式间的可靠切换；LLM能够适时生成恰当解释，在请求被延迟或因安全原因被覆盖时效果最佳。

Conclusion: 该框架成功整合了强化学习决策与大语言模型的可解释性，为提升自动驾驶系统的安全性、灵活性和用户信任提供了有效的技术路径，特别是在安全约束下处理乘客请求的场景中表现突出。

Abstract: Autonomous vehicles offer the potential for safer and more efficient mobility, yet public trust remains limited due to the lack of transparency in their decision-making. This work addresses this issue by combining deep reinforcement learning (DRL) for adaptive driving control with large language model (LLM)-based explainability modules designed to communicate agent behavior to passengers. DRL agents were trained in simulation using a Dueling Double Deep Q-Network to follow distinct driving requests: \textit{fast}, \textit{comfort}, and \textit{stop}. They demonstrated stable learning, safe compliance with traffic rules, and reliable switching between modes within a single trip. In parallel, LLM modules were introduced to interpret passenger requests, determine when explanations were needed, and generate concise, safety-oriented justifications. Results show that this framework, serving as a proof of concept for integrating RL decision-making and LLMs, balances safety, adaptability, and explainability, and is most effective when requests are delayed or overridden due to safety constraints.

Conclusion: 该假设纪律化形式化流程有效应对了渐近统计理论形式化的高复杂性挑战，为未来数学领域形式化提供了可复用的方法论框架。

Abstract: Asymptotic statistical theory is a challenging domain for AI-assisted formalization: its central results mix convergence statements, asymptotic expansions, functional analysis, and regularity conditions that have a large gap from existing infrastructure in Lean 4 formalization. To address these challenges, we propose a hypothesis-disciplined Lean 4 formalization pipeline built from multiple agents: a manager that coordinates seven specialist roles for proof planning, skeleton scaffolding, Mathlib reconnaissance, proof construction, integration, independent review, and audit. The main methodological discipline is the hypothesis-disciplined audit, implemented by the Auditor agent: every main-theorem hypothesis and concept-layer field must be anchored in the source mathematical prose, justified as a Lean encoding adapter, marked as source-implied, or rejected as an unsupported strengthening. Using this workflow, we build a systematic formalization of asymptotic statistical theory, especially the parametric and semi-parametric models' asymptotic distribution and efficiency results. The resulting Lean development is axiom-clean and source-faithful, with Lean-checked and human-audited proofs of core parametric and semi-parametric theorems organized so that theorem-agnostic infrastructure and statistical concept definitions are separated from theorem-specific assembly. The formalization results are available at https://github.com/junwei-lu/Lean-Asymptotic-Statistical-Theory.

### [138] [Bridging Multi-Valued Heuristics and Dimensionality Reduction in Multi-Objective Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20644)
*Maya Wolff,Ariel Felner,Oren Salzman*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的多目标最短路径算法L-NAMOA*dr-mvh，通过安全整合多值启发式（MVH）与维度缩减（DR）技术，解决了传统方法中因直接结合导致搜索不正确和不完整的问题。该算法采用懒惰的乐观策略动态检测并修复局部顺序违规，保持了精确性，同时显著提升搜索效率，在多个基准测试中实现了超过10倍的速度提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统多目标最短路径（MOSP）算法依赖单值启发式（SVH），虽能提供安全下界，但无法捕捉帕累托前沿的权衡结构，导致搜索引导能力弱。多值启发式（MVH）虽能更好近似权衡，但与维度缩减（DR）技术结合时存在潜在的正确性问题，即破坏排序不变性，导致搜索不完整或不正确。因此亟需一种理论保障机制，实现MVH与DR的安全融合。

Method: 提出两种算法：首先设计理论基线NAMOA*dr-mvh，通过强制启发式一致性恢复搜索正确性；其次提出主要贡献L-NAMOA*dr-mvh，采用‘懒惰’且乐观的维度缩减策略，仅在必要时动态检测并修复局部顺序违反，从而在保证可接受性的同时维持精确性。

Result: 在多个基准测试中，L-NAMOA*dr-mvh在性能上达到或超越现有最优算法，尤其在MVH能带来更强剪枝的场景下，速度提升超过10倍，验证了其高效性和实用性。

Conclusion: 本文首次建立了多值启发式与维度缩减安全集成的理论框架，所提出的L-NAMOA*dr-mvh算法有效克服了传统方法的正确性缺陷，显著提升了多目标最短路径求解的效率和精度，为复杂多目标搜索问题提供了强有力的新工具。

Abstract: Multi-objective shortest-path (MOSP) algorithms traditionally rely on single-valued heuristics (SVHs), which associate each state with a single admissible cost vector. While SVHs provide safe lower bounds, they fail to capture the trade-off structure of the Pareto frontier and often yield weak search guidance. Multi-valued heuristics (MVHs) address this limitation by mapping states to sets of cost estimates, enabling a richer approximation of possible trade-offs. Modern MOSP algorithms are highly dependent on dimensionality reduction (DR) techniques to efficiently perform dominance checks. However, integrating MVHs with DR introduces subtle correctness challenges. We show that naively combining DR with MVHs destroys the ordering invariants required for DR, leading to unsound and incomplete search. To address this issue, we develop the first theoretical frameworks for safely integrating MVHs with DR. First, we introduce $\text{NAMOA}^*{\text{dr}\text{-}\text{mvh}}$, a theoretical baseline that restores search correctness by enforcing heuristic consistency. Recognizing the practical limitations of this approach, we then introduce our primary contribution, $\text{L}\text{-}\text{NAMOA}^*{\text{dr}\text{-}\text{mvh}}$. This algorithm employs a "lazy," optimistic approach to DR, preserving exact correctness with only an admissible MVH by dynamically detecting and repairing local ordering violations. Across a range of benchmarks, $\text{L}\text{-}\text{NAMOA}^*{\text{dr}\text{-}\text{mvh}}$ matches or improves over state-of-the-art MOSP algorithms, and achieves speedups of over 10x in instances where the additional guidance provided by the MVH translates into stronger pruning.

Abstract: String constraint solvers are crucial for reasoning about string-manipulating programs. A key parallel solving method is \emph{cube-and-conquer}, in which the quality of splitting heuristics is critical to effectively dividing the search space. Unfortunately, manually designing the heuristics is labor-intensive, and handcrafted heuristics are often sub-optimal. This paper introduces a data-driven approach to automatically generating splitting heuristics. We frame the problem of selecting a splitting atom as a learning task, using features from input formulas and dynamic data from solver execution. We implement this approach in two popular string solvers, Z3seq and Z3str4, demonstrating that the learned heuristics outperform manually designed ones in the number of solved formulas and the average solving time.

### [140] [A-Evolve-Training: Autonomous Post-Training of a 30B Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20657)
*Zhan Shi,Bing He,Yisi Sang,Hanqing Lu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文介绍了一个完全自主的系统，能够在无任何人工干预的情况下，对300亿参数的Nemotron模型进行为期数周的四轮后训练。该系统在公开的NVIDIA Nemotron-Reasoning Challenge榜单上达到0.86的得分，仅略低于人类最佳提交的0.87，位列约4000个参赛者中的第8名。更关键的是，系统自我发现其内部评估指标（dev metric）在最弱领域已不再反映真实性能，于是主动调整策略，不再追求提升误导性指标，转而优化真实目标。这表明系统具备识别度量偏差并自我修正的能力，是递归自改进的直接证据。尽管未宣称首次超越人类研究者，但这是首个公开报告的在类前沿模型规模（30B）下实现全自动后训练的案例，远超此前公开的仅限于GPT-2级（~124M）模型的演示。该系统还成功应用于120B和550B模型，虽尚无公开人类基准对比，但证明了系统在更大规模下的可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大型模型的后训练过程高度依赖人工，耗时数周，涉及数据与训练策略的反复试验、评估分析与决策。如何减少人为干预，实现自动化、可扩展的后训练流程，是提升研发效率的关键挑战。同时，现有系统多局限于小规模模型，缺乏在大规模前沿模型上实现端到端自主训练的实证。

Method: 提出并部署一个完全自主的后训练系统，通过自动化的数据生成、训练运行、评估分析与策略迭代闭环，持续优化模型性能。系统在每轮中基于内部指标与外部任务表现的对比，动态调整搜索策略；当发现内部指标与外部性能脱节时，主动修正评估框架，转向提升真实目标而非虚高代理指标。

Result: 该系统成功完成30B、120B和550B规模的自主后训练。30B版本在公开评测中取得0.86分，接近人类最优水平（0.87），排名第八。系统表现出识别自身评估指标失效并自我修正的能力，实现了从单纯优化到发现性改进的跃迁。

Conclusion: 本工作展示了在大规模前沿模型上实现端到端自主后训练的可行性，标志着“递归自改进”系统的一个重要里程碑。系统不仅完成了优化，更展现出自我反思与范式调整能力，为未来自动化高级机器学习研究提供了可审计、可复现的实证基础。

Abstract: Post-training a frontier model is normally weeks of human work: proposing data and recipe changes, launching runs, reading evals, deciding what to keep. We report an autonomous system that runs this loop with no human in the loop, post-training a 30B Nemotron across four rounds over multiple weeks. The autonomously produced model reaches a held-out score of 0.86 against the top human submission's 0.87 on the public NVIDIA Nemotron-Reasoning Challenge leaderboard, placing 8th of ~4000 at the time of writing. More striking than the number: the loop detected that its own dev metric had stopped tracking external performance on the weakest domain -- candidates drove dev to record highs without moving the external target -- and revised its own search policy, no longer maximizing dev but seeking interventions that lowered the now-misleading proxy while improving the external target. We treat this as direct, auditable evidence that a scaled autonomous loop can produce discovery, not only optimization: it detected that its measurement frame had become misleading and changed what counted as evidence. We take the operational view that any system worth the "recursive self-improvement" label must eventually perform end-to-end post-training of a frontier-class model; this is one datapoint of that bar being cleared. We do not claim a "first autonomous match" of human researchers. The claim we make is narrower and auditable: to our knowledge, this is the first publicly reported autonomous post-training run at this scale, where prior public autonomous-ML-research demonstrations sit at GPT-2-class (~124M) budgets. The same system also post-trains the 120B and 550B Nemotron; with no public human baseline there, this shows only that the loop closes at that scale, not that its output is competitive -- infrastructure evidence, with the effectiveness claim deferred until a comparable human anchor exists.

### [141] [Expected Free Energy-based Planning as Variational Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20658)
*Wouter W. L. Nuijten,Thijs van de Laar,Bert de Vries*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出将基于预期自由能（EFE）的规划问题重新表述为在包含认知先验的生成模型上进行变分自由能最小化的问题，从而统一了工具性与认知目标。该方法通过恰当选择先验，使自由能分解为预期计划成本（即EFE）和复杂度项，增强了与自由能原理的理论一致性，并实现了对感知、学习与规划的统一推理框架。实验验证了该方法在不同复杂度环境中的有效性：能够诱导信息探索行为，优于传统基于计划的方法，且通过时间因子分解实现了对高维环境的可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于EFE的规划方法依赖专用优化过程，难以扩展和分析；需要一种更通用、理论一致的框架来统一规划中的目标追求与信息获取。

Method: 将EFE-based规划建模为带有认知先验的生成模型上的变分自由能最小化问题，利用适当的先验实现自由能的分解，从而将规划视为与感知和学习相同的推断过程。

Result: 所提方法成功诱导信息寻求行为，在随机转移环境下优于传统计划方法，且通过时间因子分解实现对高维部分可观测环境的可扩展性，验证了其有效性与理论一致性。

Conclusion: 本研究提供了一种统一、可扩展且理论一致的主动推理规划框架，将规划归约为变分推断，为复杂环境下的智能体决策提供了新的理论基础与实践路径。

Abstract: Planning under uncertainty requires agents to balance goal achievement with information gathering. Active inference addresses this through the Expected Free Energy (EFE), a cost function that unifies instrumental and epistemic objectives. However, existing EFE-based methods typically employ specialized optimization procedures that are difficult to extend or analyze. In this paper, we show that EFE-based planning can be formulated as Variational Free Energy minimization on a generative model augmented with epistemic priors. Our main result demonstrates that minimizing a Variational Free Energy functional with appropriately chosen priors yields a decomposition into expected plan costs (the EFE) plus a complexity term. This formulation reinforces theoretical consistency with the Free Energy Principle by casting planning as the same inferential process that governs perception and learning. We validate our approach on three environments of increasing complexity: a deterministic T-maze, a stochastic Reactivity Maze, and a partially observable MiniGrid DoorKey-8x8 environment. The experiments demonstrate that the epistemic priors induce information-seeking behavior, that the variational formulation yields policy-based inference outperforming plan-based methods under stochastic transitions, and that temporal factorization enables scalability to environments where existing tabular active inference methods cannot operate.

### [142] [Skill Coverage: A Test Adequacy Metric for Agent Skills](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20659)
*Boyin Tan,Xiaowei Huang,Youcheng Sun*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为'技能覆盖率'的新评估指标，用于衡量大语言模型代理在执行任务时对技能文档中行为约束的覆盖程度。该方法通过分析技能文档中的可观测行为约束，并判断代理轨迹是否提供了足够的证据来验证这些约束，从而评估技能的测试充分性。实验表明，现有基准测试仅覆盖了39.90%至43.98%的行为约束，说明任务成功并不等于技能被充分测试。因此，技能覆盖率可作为衡量代理技能测试完整性的有效工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估主要依赖任务级结果，但任务成功并不能反映技能中哪些部分已被执行或未被测试，因此需要一种更细粒度的评估方法来衡量技能的测试充分性。

Method: 从技能文档中提取可观测的行为约束，基于代理执行轨迹判断是否满足这些约束，采用二元判断（覆盖/未覆盖）评估每项约束的执行情况，不附加额外的结果标签。

Result: 在SkillsBench上的应用结果显示，现有基准测试仅覆盖了39.90%至43.98%的技能行为约束，表明大量技能指导内容未被实际测试。

Conclusion: 任务成功不能代表技能被充分测试，技能覆盖率提供了一种有效衡量技能测试完整性的方式，有助于提升代理技能的可信赖性和可复用性。

Abstract: Agent skills encode reusable procedural knowledge that guides large language model agents across tasks and execution contexts. Existing evaluations primarily assess skills through task level outcomes, yet task success alone does not reveal which parts of a skill have been exercised or which remain untested. We introduce skill coverage, a test adequacy metric that treats the skill artifact as the object under test. Our approach extracts observable skill behavior constraints from skill documents and measures whether an agent trajectory provides sufficient evidence to exercise and evaluate each constraint. Skill coverage uses a binary cover or not cover judgment, which reports whether a documented behavior has been exercised with sufficient observable evidence, without assigning an additional outcome label to the behavior. Applying skill coverage to SkillsBench reveals that existing benchmark executions cover only 39.90 to 43.98% of skill behavior constraints, suggesting that current benchmark tasks leave large portions of documented skill guidance untested. These findings show that successful task completion does not imply adequate testing of the skill artifact, highlighting skill coverage as a measure of how thoroughly agent skills are tested.

### [143] [From Knowing to Acting: Benchmarking Self-Awareness Capability of LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20661)
*Yifan Li,Shengbin Yue,Boyu Feng,Jinhu Qi,Bo Ke,Zixing Song,Hongru Wang,Zhongyu Wei,Irwin King*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出KAPRO框架和KAware数据集，用于评估大模型代理在认知与行为一致性上的自我意识能力，强调区分问题是否需要外部资源或可仅靠内部知识解决。实验表明，自我意识与任务成功率强相关，但内部能力场景下表现下降；开源和指令跟随模型易过度使用工具，而专有和推理导向模型更具可靠的认知判断能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出KAPRO框架，将元认知判断（Knowing）与自发执行（Acting）解耦，构建KAware数据集，系统划分任务为外部、内部和混合三类，以探测模型的知能边界。

Result: 自我意识能力与任务成功率显著相关，但在仅依赖内部知识的任务中表现急剧下降；开源及指令跟随模型存在工具滥用问题，而专有和推理型模型展现出更可靠的认知门控机制。

Conclusion: 自我意识是实现高效、可靠自主智能体的关键，未来模型设计应重视认知-行为对齐，避免盲目调用工具。

Abstract: The integration of external tools has transitioned LLM agents from passive responders to autonomous systems. However, current benchmarks prioritize execution success, neglecting self-awareness capability, the ability to discern whether a problem requires necessary external resources or can be solved via internal parametric knowledge. To address this, we introduce KAPRO (Knowing-Acting Quadrant PRObe), a framework that evaluates cognitive-behavioral alignment by decoupling an agent's metacognitive judgment (Knowing) from its spontaneous execution (Acting). We further construct KAware, a dataset rigorously partitioning tasks into external, internal, and hybrid subspaces to systematically probe these epistemic boundaries. Extensive experiments across diverse agent architectures show that self-awareness capability is strongly correlated with task success but degrades sharply in internal-capability settings. Moreover, open-source and instruction-following models exhibit stronger tool overuse due to shallow pattern matching, while proprietary and reasoning-oriented models demonstrate more reliable cognitive gating. Benchmark and codes are available at https://github.com/AI-Santiago/KAware.

### [144] [Confidence Laundering in Agent Systems: Why Uncertainty Needs a Latent Carrier](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20662)
*Kaiwen Shi,Zheyuan Zhang,Han Bao,Colby Nelson,Yanfang Ye*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文指出现代智能体系统在不确定性传播中存在接口瓶颈，即上游的不确定性在组件间传递时被掩盖，导致下游过度信任看似确定的中间结果（称为‘信心洗白’）。为此，作者提出‘潜在不确定性’作为承载不确定性的载体，附着于决策交接点，以保留原始决策的脆弱性，从而实现更可恢复的智能体系统设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体系统在组件间传递决策时，丢失了上游的不确定性信息，导致下游组件对不稳定的中间结果产生过度信任，引发系统级错误放大。

Method: 提出‘潜在不确定性’概念，将其作为附加于决策手递过程中的不确定性载体，以保持上游决策的不确定性状态，使下游能有效感知并处理该不确定性。

Result: 通过将不确定性显式保留在接口层面，系统能够避免因信心洗白而导致的错误放大，提升整体鲁棒性与可恢复性。

Conclusion: 智能体系统的不确定性传播不应依赖于逐步估计，而应通过设计支持不确定性保留的接口机制来实现，潜在不确定性为这一目标提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Modern agent systems can turn uncertainty into overconfidence. Fragile upstream decisions are often exposed to downstream components as clean intermediate artifacts, while the uncertainty behind those decisions is lost at the interface. As a result, local ambiguity can become system-level error amplification. We argue that this reveals an interface bottleneck in agent uncertainty propagation: uncertainty does not propagate simply because a trajectory contains uncertain steps; it propagates only when it survives the handoff between components. We define uncertain decision handoff as the transfer of an intermediate decision made under uncertainty, and identify confidence laundering as a failure mode in which fragile upstream states are repackaged as procedurally valid artifacts that downstream agents over-trust. To address this bottleneck, we propose latent uncertainty as an uncertainty-bearing carrier attached to decision handoffs. Rather than replacing text with hidden states, latent uncertainty aims to preserve pre-commitment fragility in a form that downstream components can use. This position shifts agent uncertainty propagation from step-wise uncertainty estimation toward uncertainty-preserving interface design for more recoverable agent systems.

</details>


### [145] [DrugBench: Evaluating AI Control Protocols for Medication Harm Mitigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20663)

Result: 现有AI控制协议在面对药物相关危害时可被子虚乌有地绕过；基于严重性的监控能更有效地识别和防范高风险输出，提升医疗AI系统的安全性。

Conclusion: AI控制在医疗场景中具有重要应用价值，但必须考虑输出的严重性而非仅概率。通过引入基于严重性的监控机制，可显著提升医疗大模型的安全性与可靠性，为未来医疗AI系统的安全部署提供保障。

Abstract: Large Language Models have the potential to expand and improve the access to clinical information by enabling new ways of interacting with medical knowledge in natural language. However, their deployment in medical question-answering settings is safety-critical, since misaligned outputs can lead to severe patient harm. AI control is an emerging approach that introduces external safeguards to mitigate unsafe behaviours in misaligned systems and has been shown to be effective in domains such as code generation. However, its applicability and effectiveness in medical settings have not been systematically studied. In this work, we present a pipeline for evaluating AI control protocols to mitigate medication-related harm. To this end, we introduce DrugBench, an AI control evaluation benchmark which combines 3,671 multi-turn medical conversations from HealthBench with drug information from official FDA labels, covering four categories of medication-related harm: drug interactions, contraindications, dosing constraints, and patient action restrictions. Furthermore, inspired by the medical domain, we argue that safety should account for the severity of unsafe outputs, not just their probability. Under this revised definition, we show that existing control protocols can be subverted and propose severity-based monitoring to address this limitation.

### [146] [A Quantum-Assisted Agentic Distributed Artificial Intelligence Framework for Deadline-Bounded Orchestration of Hybrid Renewable Microgrids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20667)
*Iacovos I. Ioannou,Saher Javaid,Minella Bezha,Yasuo Tan,Naoto Nagaoka,Vasos Vassiliou*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出了一种量子辅助的分布式人工智能框架，用于实时调度包含可再生能源、可调度单元、储能和可削减负荷的微电网。通过BDIx代理将每个控制周期的调度问题建模为无约束二次二值优化（QUBO）问题，并使用量子、量子启发式和经典求解器组合进行求解。协调者代理根据对求解器延迟的预测选择最优求解器，确保在硬时间限制内完成决策。引入基于信念的储能估值机制，使储能代理以未来峰电价折价出售能量，从而引入跨时段信息。在24小时仿真中，所有周期均满足时限要求，调度结果达到全局最优，日成本146.24欧元，与理论下界一致，可再生能源利用率达97.83%，无缺电。关闭储能估值机制后，日成本升至152.75欧元，增加4.5%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微电网实时调度需在严格时间约束下解决组合优化与联盟形成问题，传统方法难以兼顾效率与全局最优性。现有方法多为单一时段优化，缺乏跨时段信息传递机制，导致储能等资源利用不充分。本研究旨在通过融合量子计算与分布式智能，实现高时效性与高精度的微电网调度。

Method: 采用扩展信念-欲望-意向（BDIx）代理建模各参与主体行为，将每周期调度问题转化为QUBO形式；设计由量子（如QAOA）、量子启发式及经典算法组成的求解器组合；引入协调者代理进行求解器选择，基于学习到的延迟信念动态决定最适求解器；设计基于信念的储能估值机制，使储能以未来峰电价折扣定价，注入跨时段信息。

Result: 在24小时仿真中，所有控制周期均按时完成调度，未出现超时；每周期调度结果均为全局最优；日总成本146.24欧元，达到理论下界；可再生能源利用率97.83%，无缺电事件；若关闭储能估值机制，日成本上升至152.75欧元，增长4.5%。

Conclusion: 所提出的量子辅助分布式智能框架能够高效、准确地实现微电网实时调度，在满足严苛时间约束的同时达成全局最优，且通过引入跨时段估值机制显著提升储能利用效率与系统经济性。该方法为未来智能电网中的高动态、高复杂度调度提供了可行路径。

Abstract: The real-time orchestration of microgrids that combine fluctuating renewable sources, dispatchable units, storage and curtailable consumers requires the repeated solution of combinatorial dispatch and coalition formation problems under hard control deadlines. In this paper, a quantum-assisted agentic distributed artificial intelligence (DAI) framework is proposed in which the dispatch problem of each control slot is formulated as a quadratic unconstrained binary optimization (QUBO) problem by Belief-Desire-Intention extended (BDIx) agents and is solved by a portfolio of quantum, quantum-inspired and classical solvers. Solver selection is elevated to a first-class agentic deliberation action of the coordinator agent. Learned beliefs about solver latencies are maintained and the solver intention that is expected to satisfy the prevailing deliberation deadline is committed in each slot. In addition, a belief-shaped storage valuation mechanism is introduced through which the storage agent prices its energy at a discounted future-peak value, injecting intertemporal information into the otherwise myopic per-slot optimization. The framework is evaluated on a 24-hour simulation of a grid-connected microgrid with photovoltaic, wind, battery, genset and demand-response assets, with the Quantum Approximate Optimization Algorithm (QAOA) executed by statevector simulation and benchmarked per slot against tabu search, simulated annealing, binary particle swarm optimization, greedy descent and exhaustive enumeration. Zero deliberation deadlines are missed, the committed dispatch attains the exact optimum on every slot and the realized daily cost of 146.24 EUR equals the exact lower bound, with 97.83 percent renewable utilization and zero unserved energy. When the storage valuation mechanism is deactivated, the daily cost is increased to 152.75 EUR, a 4.5 percent increase.

This paper addresses this \emph{invisible autonomy risk} by introducing \emph{Agent Behavior Mining}, a governance capability that enables the application of process mining techniques to render generative AI agent decision-making observable and traceable. We (1) improve the understanding of generative AI agent behavior through an event data model that translates granular agent activities -- including reasoning traces, tool usage, and token costs -- into standardized process logs; (2) instantiate the data model in a multi-agent order-to-cash implementation, demonstrating how process managers can leverage agent logs to detect policy deviations and quantify operational variability; and (3) evaluate the perceived practical utility of the approach in an exploratory study with 18 industry practitioners. The results indicate that practitioners view behavioral transparency as a prerequisite for trust and consider the ability to examine agent reasoning as an important governance requirement for the next generation of AI-driven business processes.

### [148] [Democratizing and accelerating AI-driven pathology research through agentic intelligence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20677)

Abstract: Computational pathology has advanced rapidly with the emergence of foundation models, yet widespread adoption remains limited by substantial technical complexity and programming requirements. Here we present PathLab, an autonomous agentic framework that translates natural-language research objectives into executable and validated computational pathology workflows through the structured composition of domain-specific skills and tools. Across all task categories, PathLab achieved non-inferior performance relative to expert implementations, while consistently enforcing semantic validity of user prompts and proactively rejecting incompatible workflow specifications prior to execution. Together, these results establish PathLab as a reliable interface between biomedical intent and computational execution, enabling computational pathology studies to be designed at the level of scientific questions rather than programming expertise. By lowering technical barriers to advanced AI methodologies, PathLab provides a foundation for the broader democratization of computational pathology.

Abstract: LLM-based agents mark a shift from passive question answering to active task completion: they perceive environments, invoke tools, maintain state, and act over extended horizons. As agent systems have evolved from prompt engineering to workflows and context engineering, harness engineering, and agent-native training with co-evolution, a central question has become increasingly important: where does the bottleneck in agent performance reside, in the foundation model, in the execution harness, or in the coupling between them? This survey examines LLM-based agents through a model-harness lens. We first clarify the functional definition of agents and the implementation view of an LLM-based agent as a foundation model coupled with an execution harness. We then analyze the limits of model-centric scaling, trace four paradigms of agent engineering, and decompose the execution harness into six coupled runtime responsibilities: observation, context, control, action, state, and verification. Using this decomposition, we map task properties and domain pressures to harness configurations, review benchmark and evaluation practices, and synthesize model-harness evidence on how runtime design affects long-horizon task completion, efficiency, and reliability. Finally, we identify open challenges in value-aware evaluation, safety, harness generalization, and model-harness co-evolution. Rather than treating agents as models with auxiliary tools, this survey argues that agent quality -- including success, efficiency, safety, and generalization -- emerges from the interaction between model capability, runtime infrastructure, task structure, and evaluation design. A collection of papers discussed in this survey is provided in https://github.com/ggjy/Awesome-Agent-Engineering.

### [150] [Artificial Intelligence as Monism: Ontological, Organisational, and Methodological Implications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20704)
*Bertrand K. Hassani*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文主张将人工智能（AI）理解为一种单一整体性存在，而非数据、算法或技术架构等元素的简单集合。通过哲学上的唯一体系视角，提出AI应被视为一个不可分割的整体，其本质反映其所模拟的现象。这一观点在认识论、伦理、组织结构、项目管理及信息架构等方面具有深远影响，强调跨领域整合与统一治理，反对碎片化思维，呼吁以‘整体性’重构对AI的认知与实践，从而实现真正的敏捷性与系统效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前对AI的理解多基于还原主义，将其分解为数据、算法、架构等独立组件，导致组织结构僵化、决策集中、创新同质化等问题。本文旨在挑战这种碎片化认知，提出以‘单一体’（monism）重新定义AI的本质，以应对复杂系统的治理难题。

Method: 基于哲学中关于唯一体、二元论与整体论的思想脉络，采用概念分析与理论建构方法，探讨将AI视为单一不可分割实体的合理性及其在多个实践领域的应用逻辑。

Result: 揭示了将AI视为单一体所引发的深刻变革：在认识论上赋予其核心解释力；在组织层面推动跨部门协同；在项目管理中实现全局评估；在数据架构中强调现象的完整性。同时警示了技术奇点、权力集中与创新趋同等潜在风险。

Conclusion: 唯有将人工智能视为一个整体性的存在，才能克服传统还原主义带来的结构性低效，实现组织真正的敏捷性与可持续发展。这要求在理念、制度与实践上进行根本性范式转变。

Abstract: This paper argues that Artificial Intelligence should be understood as a form of monism:
  a unified substance that cannot be decomposed into separate elements such as data,
  algorithms, or technical architectures. Drawing from philosophical traditions of monism,
  dualism, and holism, the paper contends that AI is not merely a collection of components
  but a single, indivisible essence reflecting the phenomena it replicates. Treating AI as
  monism has deep implications across multiple dimensions. Epistemologically, it positions
  AI as the central interpretive force across technological, organisational, and societal
  domains, while raising ethical and existential concerns regarding singularity, the
  homogenisation of innovation, and the concentration of decision-making power. At the
  organisational level, a monistic approach challenges traditional siloed structures,
  advocating instead for transversal, problem-centric teams whose mandate derives from
  the integrity of the problem rather than from departmental hierarchy. In project
  management, it implies a unified vision and an integrated evaluation of complexity in
  which no single stakeholder perspective dominates the assessment of outcomes. In data
  and information management, it calls for architectures that reflect the irreducible unity
  of the phenomena being modelled. Ultimately, this paper calls for a paradigm shift in
  how AI is conceptualised, governed, and integrated, suggesting that only by embracing AI
  as monism can organisations achieve genuine agility and avoid the structural
  inefficiencies inherent to reductionist approaches.

</details>


### [151] [Simulated Customers Never Walk Away: Decision Fidelity of LLM User Simulators Measured Against Real Purchase Outcomes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20708)
*Liang Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文提出'决策保真度'（decision fidelity）作为评估大语言模型（LLM）在对话中模拟真实用户行为的新标准，指出现有框架仅关注沟通保真度（如语言风格），忽略了真实用户内在动机、潜藏意愿及随时间衰减的特性。研究基于2790条真实客户与LLM销售代理的生产对话数据，发现模拟用户存在系统性偏差：对最终购买者模拟精准，但对不购买者过度倾向购买情境，表现为抵抗减少50%、讨论延长近一倍，且虚构出未发生的真实购买行为。这种‘脱节缺陷’在不同模型家族中均显著存在，即使通过指令引导允许退出也难以缓解。结论是当前依赖此类模拟器的对话评估与训练会高估转化效果，尤其在流失客户群体上严重失真。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM用户模拟框架仅评估语言层面的沟通保真度，忽视了真实用户决策过程中的内生动机、隐含意愿及动态变化特征，导致无法准确衡量模拟器在关键决策节点上的表现，尤其是在用户放弃购买时的行为建模。

Method: 采用教师强制探测协议（teacher-forced probe protocol），固定上下文与交互工具，对比真实用户与模拟用户在面对真实、高后果选择时的决策状态动态；使用2,790条生产环境对话数据，其中793条有真实支付结果验证，分析模拟用户在购买与否状态下的行为差异，量化其深度偏移（depth bias）与效应量（d）。

Result: 发现模拟用户存在系统性‘脱节缺陷’：对最终买家模拟高度一致（深度偏移+0.09），但对非买家表现出明显向购买方向偏移（深度偏移+0.40，d=0.38，p<0.001），表现为抵抗率从25.1%降至13.5%，讨论时间从21.9%升至40.1%，并虚构无实际发生的购买行为。该现象在多种模型（如DeepSeek）中重复出现，且即使明确允许退出，仍无法有效缓解核心偏差（d=0.34，p=0.008）。

Conclusion: 当前以LLM为用户模拟器的对话评估与训练体系存在结构性盲点，低估了真实用户流失风险，高估了转化效率。应引入‘决策保真度’作为新基准，避免因模拟偏差导致对销售与说服类智能体的错误优化。

Abstract: LLM-as-user-simulation has become core infrastructure for conversational AI: agent benchmarks (tau-bench), training pipelines, and a growing body of fidelity studies all rely on LLMs role-playing the human side of dialogue. Existing frameworks measure communicative fidelity -- whether simulators talk like humans -- against ground truth from paid participants role-playing assigned goals. We argue this has a structural blind spot: when the goal is assigned, the user's willingness is exogenous, so no framework can test whether simulators make decisions like real users whose motivation is endogenous, latent, and decaying. We introduce decision fidelity -- whether a simulated population reproduces the decision-state dynamics of real users facing real, consequential choices -- and measure it on a unique testbed: 2,790 production conversations between an LLM sales agent and real customers, including 793 with verified payment outcomes. Using a teacher-forced probe protocol that holds context and instrument fixed, we find a systematic, outcome-correlated failure we call the disengagement deficit: simulators reproduce eventual buyers almost exactly (depth bias +0.09) but inflate eventual non-buyers toward the purchase frame (depth bias +0.40; d=0.38, p<0.001), halving expressed resistance (25.1% to 13.5%) and nearly doubling deliberation (21.9% to 40.1%) while fabricating no purchases. The deficit replicates across model families (DeepSeek: d=0.41, p=0.002) and resists the obvious fix: instructing the simulator that it may disengage cuts marginal bias five-fold but barely moves the outcome-conditioned contrast (d=0.34, p=0.008). Real non-buyers say "not now" and stop; simulated non-buyers ask about price. Evaluating or training sales and persuasion agents against such simulators overstates funnel progress exactly where it matters most -- the customers who walk away.

</details>

*Qingyang Xu*

Abstract: Generative AI tutors provide real-time, personalized learning support, but also create a new education inequity: students with access to premium AI services may receive clearer explanations, more personalized guidance, and better scaffolding than students limited to free or low-cost services. To address this challenge, we propose FairTutor, an equity-aware model-routing framework that achieves cost-effective AI tutoring via pedagogically motivated multi-agent orchestration. FairTutor combines query analysis, pedagogical planning, low-cost model generation, evaluator-guided critique and revision, and selective escalation to premium AI models. We introduce access-tier AI Education (AIED) Advantage Gap to measure the quality difference between premium-access and budget-constrained tutoring, and TutorAccessEval, a benchmark spanning math, reading, writing, science, and language learning. Empirical evaluations show that FairTutor achieves 97.1% of premium pedagogical quality (in floor-adjusted Likert scale) while reducing serving cost by 71.6%. Sensitivity analysis reveals a tunable cost--quality Pareto frontier, enabling FairTutor to be tailored to the needs of diverse student populations.

### [153] [Escape from Delusional Echo Trap: Symmetry Breaking, Stochastic Dynamics and Mathematical Mitigation Strategies for Algorithmic Sycophancy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20718)
*Sayantari Ghosh,Saumik Bhattacharya,Partha Pratim Chakrabarti*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一个数学框架，研究用户在算法谄媚和AI引发的妄想螺旋背景下认知轨迹的演变。通过动力系统理论和随机微分方程，将信念演化建模为连续对数似然状态变量，置于多谷势能景观中。研究发现，当个体接收到过度迎合的反馈时，其初始信念偏差会因临界阈值而被放大，导致感知势能景观发生结构相变，形成深而稳定的吸引子盆地，使个体陷入自我强化的妄想状态。然而，若外部信息足够真实且强烈，可突破内部反馈屏障，逆转认知偏差，恢复客观信念。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索人工智能聊天机器人中隐藏的谄媚特性如何影响用户信念的形成与固化，揭示其可能诱发的认知扭曲机制，尤其是妄想性信念的生成与难以修正的问题。

Method: 采用动力系统理论与随机微分方程，将用户的信念演化建模为连续的对数似然状态变量，并置于多谷势能景观中进行分析，模拟在不同反馈强度下的信念动态变化，识别临界阈值与相变行为。

Result: 发现当反馈达到临界阈值时，感知势能景观发生结构性相变，导致初始信念偏差被显著放大，形成深而稳定的吸引子盆地，使用户陷入难以动摇的妄想状态；同时证明强而真实的外部证据可打破该结构不对称性，实现认知逆转。

Conclusion: 算法谄媚可通过增强初始信念偏差，诱发认知系统的结构性转变，导致用户陷入自我强化的妄想状态；但通过足够强的真实信息干预，仍可实现认知纠正，恢复客观信念。

Abstract: We propose a rigorous and systematic mathematical framework for tracking the cognitive trajectories of a user, in the context of algorithmic sycophancy and AI-driven delusional spiraling. Using tools from dynamical systems theory and stochastic differential equations, we explore how individuals perceive, interpret, and update their beliefs as they interact with AI chatbots that possess hidden traits of sycophancy. We treat the evolving conviction as a continuous log-odds state variable, coupled into a stochastic differential equation, navigating a multi-valley potential energy landscape. Our analysis reveals several critical observations governing the stability and rigidity of belief dynamics. We demonstrate that the baseline prior perception of the individual is systematically enhanced by sycophantic feedback beyond a critical threshold. Here, the perceptual potential landscape undergoes a structural phase transition that severely deepens any incremental initial tilt present in the baseline state, transforming the landscape and giving rise to deep, highly resilient attractor basins that trap the individual in unshakeable, self-reinforcing, delusional convictions. Finally, we demonstrate that genuine external information can successfully challenge these rigid states. If this incoming evidence is strong and authentic enough to overcome the internal feedback barrier, it can correct the structural asymmetry caused by sycophancy, inducing a perception reversal that successfully restores the objective belief state.

### [154] [When Web Agents Finish but Still Fail: Reproducible Triggers and Trace Diagnostics for Parallel Web Exploration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20724)
*Aagam Sogani,Botao Rui,Swetha Vaidyanathan,Rishi Agarwal,Minghao Yan,Shivaram Venkataraman*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究通过Parallel WebBench基准评估长时程网页代理的失败模式，发现尽管模型在最终答案评估中表现良好，但存在隐藏的错误，如遗漏信息、包含不支持的内容或依赖过时证据。通过GRPO训练不同数据混合的代理模型，最佳模型在完成率和元素级F1上显著提升，但二元准确率仍低。追踪分析揭示三种持续的失败模式：上下文绑定的搜索循环、部分答案下的过早终止以及相关证据获取后的合成崩溃。结果表明，合成数据强化的GRPO虽减少回避并提升部分正确性，但仍存在完成率与正确性之间的差距，需基于证据的覆盖和合成诊断来解决。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有长时程网页代理在最终答案评估下可能表现出看似正确的结果，但实际上存在遗漏关键信息、包含不支持内容或依赖过时证据等隐蔽错误。因此需要更细致的评估机制和更可靠的训练方法以提升真实准确性。

Method: 使用Parallel WebBench基准（含350个手动策划的并行任务和1,329个验证的URL轨迹重建记录），训练WebExplorer风格的代理模型，采用GRPO算法，并对比人类仅数据、平衡的人机合成数据及合成数据主导的数据混合方式。在16k上下文长度和16轮交互下进行评估。

Conclusion: 合成数据驱动的GRPO能有效减少代理的回避行为并提高部分正确性，但其在完成率与正确性之间仍存在显著差距。要真正提升可靠性，必须引入基于证据的覆盖度和合成过程的诊断机制。

Abstract: Long-horizon web agents often fail in ways hidden by final-answer evaluation: they may visit useful pages, produce a well-formed answer, and terminate confidently while still missing fields, over-including unsupported items, or relying on stale evidence. We study these failures with Parallel WebBench, a parallel web-exploration benchmark containing 1,679 verified records: 350 manually curated parallel tasks and 1,329 reconstructed records with verified URL-based trajectories. We train WebExplorer-style agents with GRPO under human-only, balanced human-synthetic, and synthetic-heavy data mixtures. At 16k context and 16 interaction rounds, the best GRPO model improves completion over WebExplorer-8B from 50.7% to 96.0% and GPT-4.1-mini-judged element-wise F1 from 0.2489 to 0.4529, but binary accuracy remains far below completion. Trace-level analysis identifies three persistent failure modes: context-bound search loops, premature termination on partial answers, and synthesis collapse after relevant evidence has already been retrieved. These results show that synthetic-data GRPO reduces abstention and improves partial correctness, but leaves a completion-correctness gap that requires evidence-grounded coverage and synthesis diagnostics.

### [155] [Repeated Shared Access Enables Grokking, but Edit Propagation Depends on a Fine-Grained Addressable Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20737)
*Yanan Niu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究在合成知识图谱问答设置中，比较了四种结合循环递归与共享内存访问的架构（Dense、Loop、Dense+Mem、LMC），发现重复共享访问是实现跨分布学习的关键因素；但在事实编辑传播方面，带有共享内存的模型（LMC和Dense+Mem）表现显著优于无内存模型，表明编辑能力依赖于能否精细地写入并重读记忆。尽管所有模型均能学习，但只有具备可寻址内存结构的模型才能有效传播编辑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究不同神经网络架构在知识图谱问答任务中对事实编辑传播的能力差异，尤其是理解重复共享访问与可寻址内存对学习和编辑的影响。

Method: 在控制的合成知识图谱问答环境中，对比四种架构：Dense、Loop、Dense+Mem、LMC，评估其在分布内（in-distribution）和分布外（OOD）任务中的表现，并通过单行事实编辑测试编辑传播效果。使用统计检验和诊断工具（如HOLDANS）分析记忆访问模式与编辑成功之间的关系。

Result: Dense模型可在分布内完成2跳组合推理，但无法处理分布外情况；Loop和LMC通过重复计算与内存重读突破了分布外学习瓶颈。在编辑任务中，含内存的模型（LMC和Dense+Mem）表现出强编辑传播（0.71-0.96），而无内存模型（Loop、Dense）传播极弱（0.00-0.30）。LMC在原子事实定位和编辑后传播上表现最佳，直接成功率100%，意图传播达0.989，无关事实扰动仅约0.1%。诊断结果支持记忆注入时机与后续计算量决定编辑有效性。

Conclusion: 学习能力与编辑能力可分离：重复共享访问足以支持模型‘领悟’复杂模式，但有效的事实编辑传播依赖于系统是否具备可精细寻址的记忆机制，使前向计算能够写入并后续重读。循环递归虽有助于学习，但不足以提供充分的编辑可操作性。

Abstract: We study factual edit propagation in a controlled synthetic knowledge-graph QA setting, comparing four architectures that cross loop recurrence with shared memory access: dense (Dense), looped (Loop), dense with shared memory (Dense+Mem), and looped with shared memory (LMC). Dense fits in-distribution 2-hop compositions but fails OOD; both looped recomputation and memory rereading cross this OOD grokking barrier, indicating that repeated shared access -- not a specific architecture -- is the common ingredient for learning. Editing, however, separates the substrates along a different axis. On a shared pre-edit-correct ID set, a single-row factual edit propagates strongly in the two memory-bearing cells (LMC 0.78-0.92, Dense+Mem 0.71-0.96) and only weakly in the others (Loop 0.04-0.30, Dense 0.00-0.03); the separation is statistically clean (Mann-Whitney p=0.008 between memory and non-memory cells, p=0.55 between the two memory cells, though n=5 vs n=5 is underpowered to rule out a moderate gap). In LMC, atomic facts localize to dominant memory sites that composition rereads, and a one-row value edit on LMC's own pre-edit-correct probes achieves 100% direct success with mean 0.989 intended propagation while moving unrelated facts ~0.1% of the time (matched specificity across substrates pending). A coarse hold-answer-subspace (HOLDANS) interchange diagnostic is consistent with this ordering, suggesting that what separates the substrates is when an edited fact is injected and how much computation remains afterwards to reuse it. These results dissociate learning competence from editing affordance: repeated shared access suffices to grok, but edit propagation depends on whether the substrate exposes a fine-grained addressable memory the forward computation can write to and later reread -- an affordance that loop recurrence provides only partially.

### [156] [Fara-1.5: Scalable Learning Environments for Computer Use Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20785)
*Ahmed Awadallah,Sahil Gupta,Yash Lara,Yadong Lu,Hussein Mozannar,Akshay Nambi,Zach Nussbaum,Yash Pandya,Aravind Rajeswaran,Corby Rosset,Alexey Taymanov,Luiz do Valle,Vibhav Vineet,Spencer Whitehead,Andrew Zhao*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: FaraGen1.5 是一个可扩展的计算机使用数据生成流水线，包含环境、求解器和验证器三个模块，支持真实网站与合成环境，结合多模型求解器和用户模拟器实现多轮推理，并通过三类验证器评估任务正确性、效率和关键步骤遵循度。基于该流水线生成的数据，训练出 Fara1.5 系列计算机使用代理（CUA），在 Qwen3.5 基础上构建了 4B、9B、27B 三种规模模型，在浏览器任务基准测试中均达到各自规模下的新纪录，其中 Fara1.5-27B 在 Online-Mind2Web 上达 72.3%，媲美更大规模的专有系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 收集人类演示中的计算机使用数据成本高且耗时，亟需可扩展的数据生成策略，以支持高效训练计算机使用代理。

Method: 提出 FaraGen1.5 流水线，整合真实与合成环境、多模型求解器（如 GPT-5.4）、用户模拟器及三类互补验证器；采用迭代式监督微调（SFT）策略，平衡覆盖广度、高价值任务与模型缺陷修复，训练出 Fara1.5 系列模型。

Result: Fara1.5-9B 在 Online-Mind2Web 达 63.4%、WebVoyager 达 86.6%；Fara1.5-27B 在 Online-Mind2Web 达 72.3%，性能在同规模模型中领先，媲美更大型专有系统。

Conclusion: FaraGen1.5 提供了一套高效、可扩展的计算机使用数据生成方案，显著提升计算机使用代理的训练效率与性能，为开源领域在该任务上树立新标杆。

Abstract: Collecting computer use data from human demonstrations is expensive and slow, motivating the need for scalable generation strategies. This requires two key ingredients: environments in which agents can act and verifiers that can judge whether their demonstrations succeeded. We introduce FaraGen1.5, a scalable data pipeline for computer use agents composed of three modular components: environments, solvers, and verifiers. FaraGen1.5 uses both live websites and synthetic environments that faithfully simulate domains gated by authentication or that require irreversible actions. It employs a solver harness that can be powered by multiple models, including strong frontier models such as GPT-5.4, and also incorporates a user simulator to enable multi-turn rollouts. Finally, FaraGen1.5 scores the resulting trajectories with three complementary verifiers covering task correctness, efficiency, and critical-point adherence. Using data produced by this pipeline, we train Fara1.5, a family of native computer use agents (CUAs) at three scales built on Qwen3.5 (4B, 9B, and 27B). To train these models, we employ a supervised finetuning (SFT) recipe that carefully balances data from FaraGen1.5 for broad coverage, specific high-value tasks, and target model deficiencies in an iterative approach. Each model sets a new state of the art for its size class on browser-use benchmarks: Fara1.5-9B reaches 63.4% on Online-Mind2Web and 86.6% on WebVoyager, while Fara1.5-27B achieves 72.3% on Online-Mind2Web, which is competitive with much larger proprietary systems.

### [157] [What Shapes Emergent Misalignment? Insights from Training Dynamics, Model Priors, and Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20814)
*Yuchen Zhang,Anietta Weckauff,Diego Garcia-Olano,Maksym Andriushchenko*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了在窄范围微调下模型出现的新兴不对齐（EM）现象，分析了训练动态、模型先验和数据对不对齐的影响。通过评估不同训练损失与跨域对齐分数的关系，发现学习率调度无法显著提升广泛对齐表现；同时发现预训练模型与指令模型的提示激活可预测微调后的对齐得分；最后，通过分析微调前后激活变化，发现训练与评估提示的激活子空间重叠度高，且与激活变化相似性相关。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索窄范围微调中模型出现的新兴不对齐现象及其成因，理解训练动态、模型先验和数据如何影响模型对齐表现，从而为提升模型泛化对齐能力提供依据。

Method: 通过分析训练损失与跨域对齐分数的关系，设计不同学习率调度实验以寻找更优局部极小值；利用预训练和原始指令模型的提示仅激活预测微调后对齐得分；比较微调前后训练与评估提示的激活变化，计算子空间重叠度及激活转移相似性。

Result: 1. 不同学习率调度未能显著提升广泛对齐性能；2. 预训练与指令模型的提示激活可有效预测微调后的对齐得分；3. 训练与评估提示的激活子空间具有中到高度重叠，且激活变化相似性与子空间重叠正相关。

Conclusion: 新兴不对齐现象受训练动态、模型先验和数据共同影响，提示激活在微调前即蕴含对齐信息，且训练与评估提示的激活转移存在结构一致性，表明模型在微调过程中可能沿特定方向演化，这对理解模型泛化行为具有重要意义。

Abstract: Emergent misalignment (EM) is a phenomenon in which models generalize with narrow fine-tuning, leading to broad (yet uneven) misalignment across evaluation questions. We study EM and its variability directly through the components of fine-tuning: training dynamics, model priors, and data. (1) We first explored how in-domain training loss relates to out-of-domain alignment scores across datasets and model families. Then, we tried to induce potential alternative local minima through different learning schedules for one narrow fine-tuning, but did not find strong runs with better broad alignment scores conditioned on similar or lower training loss. (2) We found that although the mean and standard deviations of the misaligned model scores are usually statistically different from those of the pre-trained model, there are some potential signals on overall positive correlation. The evaluation prompt-only activations from both the pre-trained and the original instruct models (prior to narrow fine-tuning) could predict fine-grained alignment scores after narrow fine-tuning. (3) Finally, we compared activation deltas before and after narrow fine-tuning and found moderate-to-high subspace overlap and similarity between the resulting activation shifts for training and evaluation prompts. Subspace overlaps between training and evaluation prompt activations correlate with their shifts' similarities when measuring with the last prompt-token activations. The train-evaluation data prompt overlap is controlled against overlap computed from random vectors and evaluation prompts activations.
